### [131] [ConSA: Controllable Sparsity in Hybrid Attention via Learnable Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18056)
*Yao Chen,Yinqi Yang,Junyuan Shang,Xiangzhao Hao,Simeng Zhang,Yilong Chen,Tingwen Liu,Shuohuan Wang,Dianhai Yu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ConSA提出了一种可学习的混合注意力分配框架，通过L0正则化和增广拉格朗日约束，在用户指定的稀疏度目标下自动优化全注意力（FA）与滑动窗口注意力（SWA）的分配。实验表明，该方法在0.6B和1.7B规模的LLM上均优于基于规则的基线，尤其在头粒度（KV-head-wise）分配时表现更优。学习到的模式将SWA置于底层，集中FA于中层连续块，揭示了内在注意力行为的细粒度谱，且该结构在不同模型规模、稀疏度和粒度下保持一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合注意力架构依赖人工规则或简单启发式方法进行FA/SWA分配，缺乏对注意力行为的深入分析。为实现更高效、自适应的注意力分配，亟需一种可学习、可控制稀疏度的自动化方法。

Method: 采用L0正则化学习二值掩码以决定每个注意力单元使用FA或SWA；通过增广拉格朗日方法强制执行指定稀疏度目标，支持层粒度或头粒度约束。

Result: 在0.6B和1.7B规模的LLM上，学习到的分配策略显著优于规则基线，头粒度分配优于层粒度分配；学习模式呈现底部用SWA、中部集中使用FA的结构，且跨模型规模、稀疏度和粒度保持稳定。

Conclusion: ConSA成功实现了对混合注意力分配的可控制稀疏学习，揭示了注意力机制中固有的层次化行为模式，为高效大模型推理提供了新的设计范式。

Abstract: Hybrid architectures combining full attention (FA) and sliding-window attention (SWA) are a promising paradigm for efficient LLM inference. However, existing methods typically rely on hand-crafted rules or simple post-hoc heuristics for FA/SWA allocation and offer limited analysis of the attention behaviors underlying these designs. We propose Controllable Sparsity in Hybrid Attention (ConSA), a framework that learns optimal FA/SWA assignment under a user-specified sparsity target. ConSA employs L0 regularization to learn binary masks selecting between FA and SWA for each attention unit, while an augmented Lagrangian constraint enforces the target sparsity at either layer or KV-head granularity. We evaluate ConSA on two LLMs at the 0.6B and 1.7B scales. Learned allocations consistently outperform rule-based baselines, with KV-head-wise allocation yielding clear gains over layer-wise allocation. The learned patterns place SWA in the bottom layers and concentrate FA into contiguous middle-layer blocks, diverging from evenly interleaved patterns in rule-based methods. This structure persists across model scales, sparsity levels, and allocation granularities, revealing a fine-grained spectrum of intrinsic attention behaviors that underlies the learned allocation.

</details>


### [132] [Security and Privacy Prompts in the Wild: What Users Ask LLMs and How LLMs Respond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18062)
*Hobin Kim,Xiaoyuan Wu,Omer Akgul,Lujo Bauer,Nicolas Christin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究基于320万条真实用户与大语言模型（LLM）的对话数据，识别出14,727个数字安全与隐私（S&P）相关提问，并将其分为九类。通过分析450个典型问题，揭示了用户在安全与隐私方面的常见需求；进一步对270个寻求建议的S&P问题进行评估，发现商业LLM（如GPT 5.5）在98%的提示中提供“足够好”的回答，显著优于开源模型（如Llama 4，仅47%）。然而，即使在高质量响应的提示中，商业模型仍存在多次运行结果矛盾的问题，可能误导用户。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于WildChat数据集（320万条真实用户-模型对话），提取并分类S&P相关提问；对450个样本进行主题分析，对270个建议型提问进行重复测试（每条提示调用10次），评估不同模型的响应质量与一致性。

Result: 商业大语言模型在大多数S&P问题上表现优异（如GPT 5.5在98%的提示中提供良好回应），但存在响应不一致问题，同一提示多次生成矛盾建议；开源模型整体表现较差（如Llama 4仅47%达到良好水平）。

Conclusion: 尽管商业大语言模型在数字安全与隐私建议方面具备较高响应能力，但其输出不一致性可能带来误导风险。未来需提升模型推理稳定性，并基于真实用户需求构建更贴近实际的S&P问答数据集。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are widely used to fulfill users' information needs; users ask LLMs about the weather, pose educational questions, and consult them for legal assistance. One particularly understudied area is digital security and privacy (S&P), where users may seek LLMs' help on how to secure their online accounts or protect their computers from cyber attacks. To the best of our knowledge, no prior study has collected or analyzed the S&P questions users ask LLMs; prior research on LLM response quality relied on expert-authored S&P misconceptions or FAQs rather than user queries. Drawing from WildChat, a dataset of 3.2M user-LLM conversations collected in the wild, our study identifies 14,727 S&P prompts and categorizes them into nine categories covering a wide range of S&P topics. From the S&P prompts, we sampled 450 and performed a thematic analysis to characterize the S&P questions users ask LLMs. Separate from the thematic analysis, we curated 270 advice-seeking S&P prompts, where users ask for recommendations, guidance, or specific S&P information. We measured LLM response quality and consistency when posing the prompt to LLMs 10 times. We found that commercial LLMs outperform open-weight models (GPT 5.5 provided "good enough" responses on 98% of prompts; Llama 4 on 47%). However, among prompts that received high-quality responses on average, commercial models sometimes produce contradictory responses across runs, risking confusing or misleading users.

### [133] [HistoRAG: Embedding Historical Methodology in Retrieval-Augmented Generation Through Critical Technical Practice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18103)
*Noah J. Kim-Baumann,Torsten Hiltmann*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出HistoRAG框架，将历史学研究原则转化为具体的架构干预措施，以解决标准RAG在解释性学科（如历史研究）中的不足。通过分离检索与生成、时间窗口化处理、以及使用LLM作为评估者来增强可解释性与可争议性。基于SPIEGELragged对1950-1979年《明镜》杂志10万余篇文章的评估显示，标准RAG存在时代术语偏差、向量相似性与相关性弱关联、关键词与语义检索结果重叠度低等问题，验证了各项干预的有效性。同时引入‘Zwischentexte’（中间文本）概念，支持LLM生成内容在学术实践中的负责任整合。该框架为其他解释性学科提供了可迁移的RAG设计范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准RAG架构和评估方法主要面向事实问答任务，不适用于历史等解释性学科，其隐含假设与学术实践相冲突。历史研究强调时间维度平衡、源材料解读与批判性分析，而现有RAG在检索与生成中缺乏对这些原则的支持，导致结果偏倚且不可解释。因此需要一种符合历史学知识论的RAG框架。

Method: 提出HistoRAG框架，包含三大核心机制：(1) 分离检索与生成，使源发现与解释解耦；(2) 时间窗口化，确保各时期资料均衡覆盖；(3) 使用大语言模型作为评判者进行后检索评估，提升相关性判断的透明度与可争议性。此外，引入双层检索（关键词+语义），并通过共享的LLM过滤器整合互补信息，并提出‘Zwischentexte’作为解释性生成文本的中间形式。

Result: 在对102,189篇《明镜》文章的评估中，验证了三项关键缺陷：(1) 使用1970年代术语无法检索1950年代文献，暴露时代词汇偏倚；(2) 向量相似性与人工相关性仅呈弱相关（Spearman rho = 0.275），说明单纯依赖向量匹配不可靠；(3) 关键词与语义检索结果几乎不重叠，证明二者应并行互补。实验表明，所提架构显著改善了检索公平性、相关性与解释性。

Conclusion: HistoRAG成功将历史学的方法论要求转化为可操作的系统设计，展示了如何将领域特定的知识论嵌入RAG架构。其核心机制不仅提升了历史研究的可解释性与可靠性，也为其他解释性学科在大规模文本处理中应用RAG提供了可复用的范式。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) is the prevailing architecture for grounding language model outputs in external evidence, yet its dominant evaluation paradigms and default configurations remain oriented toward factual question-answering. For interpretive disciplines such as historical studies, RAG embeds assumptions that conflict with scholarly practice. We introduce HistoRAG, a framework that translates historiographical principles into concrete architectural interventions. Separated retrieval and generation decouples source discovery from interpretation, temporal windowing enforces balanced source representation across the research period as a methodological requirement of historical inquiry, and LLM-as-judge evaluation makes relevance judgments transparent and contestable. We evaluate these interventions using SPIEGELragged, applied to 102,189 articles from Der Spiegel (1950-1979). Each intervention addresses a measurable deficiency in standard RAG: era-specific vocabulary retrieves zero chunks from the 1950s when using 1970s terminology, evidence of the temporal skew that motivates windowing; vector similarity and LLM-assessed relevance correlate only weakly (Spearman rho = 0.275), motivating post-retrieval evaluation; and keyword-based and semantic retrieval surface largely disjoint source pools, motivating an architecture in which both operate as complementary retrieval layers under a shared LLM evaluation filter. We also introduce the concept of Zwischentexte (intermediate texts that function as interpretive proposals rather than findings) as a framework for responsible integration of LLM-generated text into scholarly practice. The architecture offers a model for how domain-specific epistemological commitments can be translated into RAG design decisions, and may transfer to other interpretive disciplines working with large corpora.

</details>


### [134] [Unintended Effects of Geographic Conditioning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18124)
*Naz Col,David M. Chan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了对话式AI系统中因用户元数据导致的地理信息泄露问题，发现即使在无地理提示的情况下，模型仍会因位置元数据而产生区域特异性输出，且这种泄露可高达基线的793倍。更值得注意的是，仅用'未知'替代地理位置仍引发高达72倍的泄露，表明用户资料框架本身即构成生成条件信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话AI系统依赖用户元数据进行本地化响应，但其引入的隐性区域偏见尚未被充分理解，亟需评估位置信息泄露对模型输出的影响。

Method: 通过在创意写作和开放式问答任务中测试多个先进大模型（如Llama 3.1-8B、Qwen3-8B、Claude Sonnet 4.6），分析其在接收地理中立提示时是否仍生成地理相关输出，并对比注入真实位置与使用占位符'Unknown'两种情形下的泄露程度。

Result: 实验结果显示，所有测试模型均表现出显著的位置泄露现象，最高达基线的793倍；即使替换为'Unknown'占位符，泄露仍提升至基线的72倍，证明用户资料框架本身具有结构性诱导作用。

Conclusion: 位置元数据不仅包含具体地理信息，其存在本身就会作为生成条件信号，诱导模型产生区域偏见。这揭示了现代对话系统在隐私与公平性方面的潜在风险，呼吁在设计中加强对元数据影响的控制与透明度。

Abstract: Modern conversational AI systems frequently rely on user metadata to localize responses, yet the unintended regional biases introduced by this hidden context remain poorly understood. In this work, we evaluate location leakage: the phenomenon where a model generates geographic references despite receiving a geographically neutral user prompt. Across both creative writing and open-ended Q&A prompts, even state-of-the-art LLMs systematically favor region-specific outputs when exposed to location metadata, with leakage spiking by up to 793 times above baseline (e.g., from 0.04% to 31.7% for Llama 3.1-8B, and 21.3% and 8.8% for Qwen3-8B and Claude Sonnet 4.6, respectively). Our analysis further shows a novel structural conditioning effect: replacing the injected location with the placeholder "Unknown" still elevates leakage by up to 72 times above baseline, demonstrating that the user profile frame itself, independent of any geographic content, acts as a generative conditioning signal.

### [135] [Learning from the Self-future: On-policy Self-distillation for dLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18195)
*Yifu Luo,Zeyu Chen,Haoyu Wang,Xinhao Hu,Yuxuan Zhang,Zhizhou Sha,Shiwei Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: d-OPSD is the first on-policy self-distillation framework designed for diffusion LLMs (dLLMs), addressing the limitations of autoregressive-centric methods. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing on-policy self-distillation (OPSD) methods are designed for autoregressive models and rely on left-to-right prefix conditioning and token-level supervision, which conflict with the arbitrary-order generation nature of diffusion LLMs (dLLMs). This limits the applicability of OPSD to dLLMs.

Method: d-OPSD reframes self-teacher construction by using self-generated answers as suffix conditioning, enabling the student model to learn from 'self future-experience'. It also shifts supervision from token-level to step-level, aligning with the iterative denoising process of dLLMs.

Result: Experiments on four reasoning benchmarks show that d-OPSD consistently outperforms RLVR and SFT baselines, achieving superior sample efficiency—requiring only about 10% of the optimization steps needed by RLVR.

Conclusion: d-OPSD opens a promising pathway for post-training diffusion LLMs by effectively adapting self-distillation to their unique generation mechanism, demonstrating strong performance with high efficiency.

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) has proven effective for post-training large language models (LLMs), yet its application to diffusion LLMs (dLLMs) remains unexplored. Existing OPSD methods are inherently autoregressive-centric. They inject privileged information via left-to-right prefix conditioning with token-level divergence supervision, a design that fundamentally conflicts with the arbitraryorder generation of dLLMs. We introduce d-OPSD, the first OPSD framework tailored for dLLMs. Our approach makes two core contributions. First, we reframe self-teacher construction by using self-generated answers as suffix conditioning, enabling the student model to learn from "self future-experience" rather than privileged prefixes. Second, we shift supervision from token-level to step-level, aligning training with the iterative denoising process of dLLMs. Experiments across four reasoning benchmarks show that d-OPSD consistently outperforms RLVR and SFT baselines with superior sample efficiency, requiring only around 10% of the optimization steps by RLVR and opening a promising pathway for dLLM posttraining. The code is available at https://github.com/xingzhejun/d-OPSD.

### [138] [Zone of Proximal Policy Optimization: Teacher in Prompts, Not Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18216)
*Byung-Kwan Lee,Ximing Lu,Shizhe Diao,Minki Kang,Saurav Muralidharan,Karan Sapra,Andrew Tao,Pavlo Molchanov,Yejin Choi,Yu-Chiang Frank Wang,Ryo Hachiuma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ZPPO, inspired by Vygotsky's zone of proximal development, enhances knowledge distillation in small-student regimes by using reformulated prompts (BCQ and NCQ) to improve learning on hard questions without violating on-policy assumptions. It uses a prompt replay buffer to iteratively refine student performance, achieving superior results across multiple scales, especially at the smallest model size.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard knowledge distillation is brittle for small students because it forces imitation of teacher logits, leading to overfitting on sharp modes and poor generalization. Reinforcement learning methods like GRPO risk policy drift when injecting teacher responses into gradients. ZPPO aims to preserve on-policy training while leveraging teacher guidance effectively.

Method: ZPPO introduces two novel prompt types: Binary Candidate-included Question (BCQ), which pairs correct and incorrect responses for discrimination, and Negative Candidate-included Question (NCQ), which aggregates student errors to expose failure patterns. A prompt replay buffer retains difficult questions until the student improves or is evicted, enabling iterative refinement within the student's 'zone of proximal development'.

Result: On Qwen3.5 models (0.8B–9B) with a 27B teacher, ZPPO outperforms both off-policy and on-policy distillation methods as well as GRPO, showing the largest improvements at the smallest model scale across a diverse 31-benchmark suite including vision-language, language, and video tasks.

Conclusion: ZPPO effectively bridges the gap between teacher guidance and student autonomy by embedding the teacher within the prompt rather than the policy gradient, enabling robust and scalable knowledge transfer—particularly beneficial for small models.

Abstract: Knowledge distillation transfers a teacher's competence to a small student but is brittle in the small-student regime: forcing the student to imitate logits from a much larger teacher concentrates it on the teacher's sharpest modes, hurting generalization on benchmark families beyond the training corpus. Reinforcement learning (RL) avoids logit imitation by training on the student's own rollouts. However, on questions where every rollout fails-yielding zero advantage and being silently discarded-injecting a stronger teacher's response into the policy gradient breaks the on-policy assumption and induces drift. We introduce Zone of Proximal Policy Optimization (ZPPO), inspired by Vygotsky's zone of proximal development, which keeps the teacher inside the prompt rather than the policy gradient. On hard questions, ZPPO constructs two reformulated prompts: a Binary Candidate-included Question (BCQ) pairs one correct teacher response with one incorrect student response as anonymized candidates the student must discriminate, and a Negative Candidate-included Question (NCQ) aggregates the student's wrong rollouts into a single prompt to surface their shared failure modes. A prompt replay buffer recirculates each hard question until it either graduates-the student's mean rollout accuracy on it reaches half- or is FIFO-evicted under finite capacity, amplifying BCQ and NCQ inside the student's current zone of proximal development. On the Qwen3.5 family at four student scales (0.8B-9B) with a 27B teacher, post-trained as vision-language models and evaluated on a 31-benchmark suite (16 VLM, 10 LLM, 5 Video), ZPPO outperforms off/on-policy distillation and GRPO, with the largest gains at the smallest scale.

</details>

*Joy Bose*

TL;DR: Darshana Graph is a large-scale corpus of over 125,000 text records from classical Hindu, Buddhist, and Jain traditions, with a unique subset of ~8,500 aligned verses across 18 commentators from five Vedanta schools and other darshanas. It enables direct cross-commentator comparison. Two analyses are presented: (1) stylometric analysis of citation density, refutation rate, and sentence complexity—revealing moderate negative correlation between citations and refutations, lineage-based increases in refutation, and genre differences in the Pali Canon; (2) a constrained LLM pipeline for extracting typed philosophical relationships using a predefined relation vocabulary and deterministic validation, which exposes cross-school disagreements but also highlights limitations when compared to embedding-based methods. The full corpus, relationship graph, and code are publicly released.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To enable systematic comparative study of interpretive traditions in Indian philosophy by providing a large-scale, cross-commentator aligned dataset that supports both stylometric and semantic relationship analysis, addressing the lack of publicly available resources at this scale and granularity.

Method: The paper constructs Darshana Graph by curating public-domain translations and aligning identical root verses across multiple historical commentators. Stylometric analysis uses quantitative metrics like citation density, refutation rate, and sentence complexity without machine learning. A constrained large language model pipeline extracts philosophical relationships using a predefined relation vocabulary and deterministic post-hoc validation.

Result: Stylometric analysis reveals moderate negative correlation between citation density and refutation rate, increased refutation in certain doctrinal lineages, and measurable genre-level variation within the Pali Canon. The LLM pipeline successfully identifies cross-school disagreement patterns but also uncovers cases where its findings contradict those from independent embedding-based analysis, indicating extraction limitations.

Conclusion: Darshana Graph provides a novel, open resource for analyzing philosophical interpretation across Indian traditions. Abstract: We introduce Darshana Graph, a corpus of over 125,000 text records spanning classical Hindu, Buddhist, and Jain philosophical traditions, drawn from public-domain and openly licensed translations of sources including the Bhagavad Gita, Brahma Sutras, principal Upanishads, the Pali Canon, and core Jain texts. Its distinctive contribution lies in a structurally unique subset of roughly 8,500 Hindu and Jain records in which the same root verse or sutra is aligned across eighteen historical commentators representing five schools of Vedanta and other darshanas, enabling direct comparison of how independent interpretive traditions read identical source material. To our knowledge, no publicly available resource provides comparable cross-commentator alignment at this scale. We present two analyses built on this corpus. First, a transparent stylometric comparison requiring no machine learning measures argumentative style through scriptural citation density, explicit refutation rate, and sentence complexity. It finds a moderate negative correlation between citation density and refutation rate, a marked increase in refutation rate across three commentators in a related doctrinal lineage, and measurable genre-level differences within the Pali Canon itself. Second, we describe a constrained large language model pipeline that extracts typed philosophical relationships between concepts using a predefined relation vocabulary and deterministic post-hoc validation. The resulting graph surfaces cross-school disagreement patterns while also revealing important extraction limitations, including cases where an independent embedding-based analysis disagrees with the graph-derived findings. We release the full corpus, extracted relationship graph, and all source code.

Abstract: Reproducing research results from papers and released code is central to scientific progress. Existing works have introduced benchmarks to evaluate whether LLM agents can assist with reproducibility, but they are difficult to scale due to their reliance on substantial manual effort for data curation and evaluation. We introduce ReproRepo, a scalable framework for reproducibility evaluation that leverages human-raised GitHub issues as naturally occurring supervision on realistic reproduction blockers. We instantiate ReproRepo on 1,149 recent machine learning papers from major conferences and evaluate four frontier model-agent configurations. Our results show that LLM agents, even without executing code, can identify many real-world reproducibility problems from paper-repository pairs: the best agent in our study, namely Codex with GPT-5.5, surfaces at least one semantically related human-reported blocker for ~90% of papers in the study. ### [141] [Variable-Width Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18246)
*Zhaofeng Wu,Oliver Sieberling,Shawn Tan,Rameswar Panda,Yury Polyanskiy,Yoon Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种非均匀宽度分配的Transformer架构——> <former，通过在早期和晚期层保持较宽、中间层变窄的方式，实现更高效的资源利用。该设计采用无参数残差重缩放机制，在不增加额外参数的情况下优化计算分布。实验表明，该模型在200M至3B参数范围内均优于同等参数量的均匀架构，降低语言建模损失，并减少22%的FLOPs、15%的KV缓存内存与I/O开销。分析显示，这种瓶颈结构导致残差流中表示形式发生质变，证明非均匀容量分配可实现更优的语言模型扩展策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer模型通常在所有层保持固定宽度，未能根据各层不同计算角色合理分配参数与计算资源，限制了模型效率与性能。为探索更高效的模型扩展方式，本文研究非均匀宽度分配对模型表现的影响。

Method: 提出> <former架构，采用\times-形状的宽度变化模式：早期和末尾层较宽，中间层较窄；使用参数无关的残差重缩放机制实现跨层特征维度匹配。通过在多尺度解码器语言模型上进行训练与评估，对比统一宽度基线模型的表现。

Result: 在200M至3B参数规模下，> <former在语言建模损失上持续优于参数匹配的均匀基线模型；整体计算量下降22%（按损失匹配缩放曲线），KV缓存内存及I/O成本减少15%；残差流中的表征差异表明该结构引入了新的表示特性。

Conclusion: 非均匀宽度分配可通过优化计算资源分布提升语言模型的性能与效率，是一种更具资源效益的模型扩展路径。

Abstract: Scaling model size, specifically depth and width, has driven significant progress in transformer-based language models. However, most architectures maintain a constant width across all layers, allocating a fixed parameter and computation budget evenly despite different layers potentially playing distinct computational roles. In this work, we empirically investigate nonuniform capacity allocation across network depth by proposing a $\times$-shaped > <former architecture. This design maintains wider early and late layers while narrowing the middle layers, utilizing a parameter-free residual resizing mechanism. Across decoder-only language models ranging from 200M to 2B parameters (dense) and 3B parameters (MoE), our > <former consistently outperforms parameter-matched uniform baselines on language modeling loss. By reducing the average layer width, this architecture also requires fewer overall FLOPs (22% reduction under fitted loss-matched scaling curves) and smaller KV cache memory and I/O cost (15% reduction). In analysis, we show that this bottleneck structure results in qualitatively different representations in residual streams. Overall, our results demonstrate that nonuniform width allocation can result in more resource-optimal scaling of language models.

</details>

### [142] [Beyond Parallel Sampling: Diverse Query Initialization for Agentic Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17209)
*Sidhaarth Murali,João Coelho,Jingjie Ning,João Magalhães,Bruno Martins,Chenyan Xiong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了代理搜索在测试时的广度扩展，发现标准并行采样因首轮查询冗余导致收益递减。为此提出DivInit方法，在首轮通过从单次调用中选取多样化的种子查询来提升并行轨迹的多样性，从而改善多跳问答性能。在五个开源模型和八个基准上均取得显著提升，平均提升5-7个百分点，且无需额外训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准并行采样在测试时扩展中存在查询冗余问题，导致多个并行轨迹检索到相似证据，降低效率。需要一种无需训练的方法来提升首轮查询的多样性，以增强后续推理效果。

Method: DivInit：在第一轮查询阶段，先从一次模型调用中生成n个候选查询，从中选择k < n个具有多样性的种子查询，作为并行轨迹的初始输入，从而减少冗余、提升信息覆盖。

Result: 在五个开放权重模型和八个基准测试中，DivInit相比标准并行采样在相同计算量下平均提升5-7个百分点，尤其在多跳问答任务中表现显著。

Conclusion: DivInit是一种无需训练的高效干预方法，能有效缓解测试时并行采样中的查询冗余问题，显著提升代理搜索性能，具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: Test-time scaling for agentic search typically increases depth (i.e., more turns and tokens per trajectory) or breadth (i.e., more parallel rollouts). Here we focus on breadth scaling, showing that standard parallel sampling yields diminishing returns, tracing this to query redundancy at the first turn. When models issue similar first queries across rollouts, the threads retrieve overlapping evidence, and subsequent turns are conditioned on this shared retrieval. We address this limitation with DivInit, a training-free intervention at the first turn. Rather than sampling k independent first queries, DivInit draws n candidates from a single call, picks k < n diverse seeds, and runs them as parallel trajectories. Across five open-weight models and eight benchmarks, DivInit consistently improves over standard parallel sampling, with average gains of five to seven points on multi-hop QA at matched compute. Code available at https://github.com/cxcscmu/diverse-query-initialization

</details>


### [143] [When Rules Learn: A Self-Evolving Agent for Legal Case Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17220)
*Mingxu Tao,Jiawei Hu,Xian Zhou,Wenpeng Hu,Jiajun Cheng,Yunbo Cao,Zhunchen Luo,Guotong Geng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需参数训练的自演化规则驱动查询重写框架，通过LLM代理在自动评估环境中迭代生成、验证和淘汰重写规则，显著提升BM25在中文法律案例检索中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管密集检索模型取得进展，但BM25仍是法律案例检索领域的强基线，因此需要一种无需训练即可增强其性能的方法，以应对法律语言复杂性和精确词汇对齐的挑战。

Method: 设计一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的代理系统，配备自动评估环境，实现规则的自动生成、组合实验规划、无效规则剔除，并利用历史反馈进行自我演化优化。

Result: 在LeCaRD-v2中文法律案例检索基准上，该框架优于非演化基线方法（包括人工设计规则和贪心规则选择），尤其在使用高容量核心LLM时表现更优；详细分析表明，LLM利用历史结果与内在规则剔除知识是实现规则集优化的关键机制。

Conclusion: 所提出的自演化框架有效提升了传统检索模型BM25在法律案例检索中的性能，证明了无需训练的规则演化策略在专业领域应用中的潜力。

Abstract: Legal case retrieval remains challenging due to the complexity of legal language and the need for precise lexical alignment between queries and relevant cases. Although dense retrieval models have achieved notable progress, empirical studies show that BM25 continues to serve as a strong baseline in this domain. It motivates us to propose a self-evolving framework for rule-driven query rewriting that enhances BM25 without any parameter training. The framework equips an LLM-based agent with an automatic evaluation environment, enabling it to iteratively create rewriting rules, plan validation experiments over rule combinations, and eliminate ineffective rules based on historical feedbacks. We evaluate our method on the Chinese legal case retrieval benchmark LeCaRD-v2. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed framework outperforms non-evolutionary baselines, including human-designed rules and greedy rule selection, particularly when powered by a highcapacity core LLM. We also conduct detailed analyses to investigate the mechanisms underlying self-evolution. Our findings reveal that LLM's capabilities to leverage previous experimental results and its intrinsic knowledge of rule elimination play critical roles in refining the rule set via self-evolution.

</details>


### [144] [SkillChain-Gym: A Benchmark for Reskilling-Aware Production-Inventory Control under Disruptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17266)
*Carlos Eduardo Sanoja*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出SkillChain-Gym基准，用于评估考虑再培训的生产-库存控制策略。该基准包含工人技能动态、认证阈值、遗忘机制和受时间预算约束的训练动作，涵盖多种可行性模式、中断场景和评估指标。通过对比不同策略在60个周期内的表现，发现训练能力策略优于纯生产策略，且维护性培训在遗忘存在时至关重要。自适应训练在可预测瓶颈时有效，而静态交叉培训则在突发冲击下表现良好。政策表现依赖于系统状态（如容量余量和遗忘率），无单一最优策略，强调基于预测的决策机制以平衡技能保险与响应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生产计划模型通常将劳动力视为外生因素，而具备技能学习和再培训的劳动力规划模型缺乏可复用的测试平台。随着技能过期、新产品需求及再培训与生产争抢工时等问题日益突出，亟需一个能同时考虑技能动态与生产调度的标准化评估框架。

Method: 设计并实现SkillChain-Gym：一个单站点的仿真环境，包含技能状态演化、硬阈值认证、技能遗忘机制、受时间预算限制的训练动作，并支持种子控制的中断情景、三种可行性模式、投影诊断、确定性重放和多维度评估指标。采用配对统计检验比较四种策略（纯生产、反应式自适应、水填式自适应、静态保险）在不同预算配置下的表现。

Result: 策略表现具有显著的制度依赖性，不存在统一最优策略。训练能力策略优于纯生产基线；即使无外部中断，遗忘也要求进行维护性培训。当瓶颈可预测时，自适应训练更优；而在突发冲击或缺勤情况下，静态交叉培训作为“保险”策略表现强劲。系统容量冗余和遗忘率是决定策略优劣的关键边界参数。

Conclusion: 应发展基于预测的动态控制器，根据环境状态决定何时购买技能保险（如静态交叉培训）或采取反应式策略。单一策略无法适应所有情况，需结合系统特征灵活选择。本研究推动了生产与人力规划融合的可复用基准建设。

Abstract: Production planning increasingly has to treat workforce capability as a decision variable: certifications lapse when skills are not maintained, new products require skills the current workforce does not hold, and reskilling competes for the same worker hours needed for production. Existing operations benchmarks usually treat labor as exogenous, while workforce-planning models with skills and learning are rarely released as reusable testbeds. We introduce SkillChain-Gym, a benchmark specification for reskilling-aware production-inventory control: a single-site environment with stylized worker skill-state dynamics, hard threshold certification, forgetting, and capacity-consuming training actions constrained by the same per-worker time budget as production. The benchmark includes seed-controlled disruption scenarios, three feasibility modes with projection diagnostics, deterministic replay, and metrics covering operations, resilience, capability growth, and training-access distribution. We evaluate production-only, reactive adaptive, water-filling adaptive, and static-insurance policies with budget variants over 60-shift horizons with paired statistical tests. The results are regime-dependent rather than a ranking. Training-capable policies dominate the production-only baseline, and maintenance training is necessary under forgetting even without disruptions. Among training-capable classes, adaptive training helps when bottlenecks are visible in the forecast, while a lean static cross-training plan, a deliberately favorable comparator whose structure encodes relevant skill contingencies, acts as strong insurance under surprise shocks and absenteeism. Capacity slack and the forgetting rate govern the boundary between these regimes. No policy class dominates across regimes, motivating forecast-driven controllers that decide when to buy skill insurance and when to react.

</details>


### [145] [Skill-Constrained Model Predictive Control for Resilient Manufacturing Supply Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17269)
*Carlos Eduardo Sanoja*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种闭环技能约束模型预测控制器，用于解决生产-库存系统中因培训决策影响未来合格人力的问题。通过在每个班次求解有限时域混合整数规划，同时优化生产、库存、缺货和培训，并引入可解释的终端价值以定价边界处的认证能力缺口。在多种模拟场景下评估该控制器，结果显示其表现依赖于具体情境：当技能或劳动力瓶颈可提前预测并有足够时间完成培训时，预测控制有效；而在突发冲击或需求-产能边界附近，静态保险策略仍具竞争力。关键发现是‘可预测性’而非‘适应性’决定预测控制是否划算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在技能受限的生产-库存系统中，合格人力取决于当前的培训决策，而培训与生产共享稀缺的人力资源。如何平衡培训与生产之间的冲突，特别是在存在技能衰减、新技能需求、劳动力波动等不确定因素时，成为核心挑战。传统方法难以应对动态变化，亟需一种能前瞻性规划且兼顾实际约束的智能控制机制。

Method: 采用基于模型预测控制（MPC）的闭环框架，在每个周期求解一个有限时域的混合整数规划问题，综合考虑生产、库存、缺货与培训决策；引入二值化预测认证状态、硬性生产准入规则及可解释的终端价值函数来反映远期能力缺口。仅执行第一阶段动作后重新规划。

Result: 实验表明，预测控制并非普遍优于其他策略。其优势仅出现在技能或劳动力瓶颈可较早预测并允许培训完成的情况下；而在突发冲击、接近需求-产能边界或存在充足预设冗余时，静态交叉培训保险策略依然表现强劲。属性分解分析揭示了认证维护、再认证和新技能获取三类行为的不同贡献。

Conclusion: 预测控制的价值不在于其自适应能力本身，而在于系统的可预测性。只有当未来瓶颈可被提前识别并留出足够时间进行培训时，预测控制才具备优势；否则，简单而稳健的静态策略往往更可靠。

Abstract: In skill-constrained production-inventory systems, the qualified human capacity available tomorrow depends on training decisions made today: production requires certified workers, certifications decay unless maintained, and training consumes the same scarce worker hours that production needs now. We study a closed-loop skill-constrained model predictive controller that, at every shift, solves a finite-horizon mixed-integer program over production, inventory, backlog, and training, with binary predicted certification, hard production eligibility, and an interpretable terminal value that prices certified-capacity gaps at the horizon boundary; only the first-period action is applied before replanning. On synthetic, seed-controlled SkillChain-Gym scenarios - announced and surprise new-skill shocks, demand shocks, absenteeism, forecast- and availability-quality modes, capacity-boundary and training-rate sweeps, and negative controls - we evaluate the controller against production-only and maintenance-only ablations, static cross-training insurance plans, and a strong reactive heuristic, under an ex-ante locked configuration and paired statistics. The result is regime dependence, not superiority: no policy class dominates. Predictive control helps when skill or labor bottlenecks are forecastable early enough for training to complete; lean static insurance remains hard to beat under surprise shocks, near the demand-capacity boundary, and wherever pre-shock slack makes insurance cheap. Attribution ablations separate certification maintenance, re-acquisition of lapsed certifications, and greenfield skill acquisition. Forecastability, not adaptivity per se, decides when predictive control pays.

</details>


### [146] [Nothing from Something: Can a Language Model Discover 0?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17289)
*Phoebe Zeng,Thomas L. Griffiths,Brenden M. Lake*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型在数学发现方面的能力，特别是其能否在训练数据之外独立发现‘零’的概念。结果表明，GPT-2规模的语言模型在无额外训练的情况下无法实现这一类外泛化，但经过数十至数百个关于‘零’的示例训练后，性能显著提升。此外，语言预训练可减少约50%的所需训练样本，表明语言能力有助于神经模型进行数学发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以简单算术为案例，评估GPT-2规模的语言模型在未见过的上下文中发现‘零’概念的能力，通过对比有无语言预训练以及不同数量训练样本下的表现进行实验。

Result: 语言模型在无额外训练时无法发现‘零’；但经过少量示例训练后表现显著提升；语言预训练可使所需训练样本减少约50%。

Conclusion: 语言能力可作为数学发现的支撑，帮助神经网络更高效地实现外分布泛化，但仅靠预训练不足以实现真正的数学创新，仍需特定任务的显式训练。

Abstract: AI systems based on artificial neural networks are being developed with aspirations of pushing the boundary of human mathematical knowledge. A key question for these systems is how much they can reach beyond their training data. Mathematical discovery requires a strong form of out of distribution generalization; the ability to hypothesize genuinely new - and potentially logically more powerful - mathematical structures. It has been hypothesized that language abilities support such generalizations in human cognition. In this work, we use simple arithmetic as a case study for examining how modern AI models could expand their mathematical horizons, evaluating whether these models can independently discover the concept of "zero". We show that We show that (1) language models of a GPT-2 size are unable to perform this generalization at test time regardless of language pretraining, but (2) models can improve substantially after training on tens or hundreds of examples of zero. Additionally, we find that language pretraining reduces the number of required examples by approximately $50\%$, showing that language abilities can scaffold mathematical discovery in neural models.

### [147] [Quantifying Consistency in LLM Logical Reasoning via Structural Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17312)
*Baishali Chaudhury,Mengdie Flora Wang,Hyunji Hayley Park,Rahul Ghosh,Sungmin Hong,Jae Oh Woo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为结构不确定性（structural uncertainty）的新框架，通过分析大语言模型在自生成推理路径中的偏好一致性来评估其推理可靠性。该方法利用模型自身对多个推理方案的成对比较，结合Bradley-Terry模型与PageRank构建排名分布，并分解为两个基于熵的分量：跨试验排名不稳定性与试验内候选模糊性。实验表明，该结构信号在逻辑和数学推理任务中补充了传统答案分散度的信息，有效识别不可靠推理实例；而在事实检索任务中信号趋于均匀，揭示出推理一致性评估失效的边界。其中，试验内模糊性与正确性正相关，而跨试验不稳定性则负相关，说明其并非通用置信度估计器，而是依赖于推理场景的逻辑一致性评估工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要依赖输出分散度来评估大语言模型的可靠性，但忽略了模型对自身推理路径的一致性判断能力。尤其在多步演绎推理中，即使答案一致，推理过程可能不稳定、矛盾或难以排序，导致可靠性误判。因此，需要一种能捕捉推理路径一致性的新机制。

Method: 提出结构不确定性框架，通过生成多个推理候选解，让模型自身进行成对偏好判断；使用Bradley-Terry模型与PageRank聚合偏好形成排名分布，并将信号分解为两个熵基分量：跨试验排名不稳定性（反映不同尝试间排名变化程度）与试验内候选模糊性（反映单次尝试中路径选择的不确定性）。

Result: 在五种大语言模型和八个基准测试上验证，结构信号与答案分散度具有互补性。在逻辑与数学推理任务中，结合两者可更准确识别不可靠实例；在事实检索任务中，结构信号趋近均匀，表明此时推理一致性评估无效。试验内模糊性与正确性正相关，跨试验不稳定性与正确性负相关。

Conclusion: 结构不确定性并非通用置信度指标，而是一种情境敏感的逻辑推理一致性评估工具，其有效性取决于任务是否具备可比较的推理路径。

Abstract: Large language models can arrive at the same answer through reasoning paths that are unstable, contradictory, or difficult to rank consistently -- a failure mode especially prevalent in multi-step deductive reasoning. Existing methods assess reliability primarily through output dispersion -- measuring how much sampled answers differ -- but this discards a complementary signal: whether the model can consistently rank competing reasoning candidates. We propose structural uncertainty, a consistency-aware framework derived from the stability of self-preference-induced rankings over sampled reasoning solutions. Given a query, we generate multiple candidate solutions and ask the model to judge pairwise preferences among its own outputs. We aggregate self-preferences into ranking distributions via Bradley-Terry modeling with PageRank, and decompose the signal into two entropy-based components: across-trial ranking instability and within-trial candidate ambiguity. Across five LLMs and eight benchmarks, structural signals provide information complementary to answer dispersion: on logical and mathematical reasoning tasks, the combination improves identification of unreliable instances, while on factual retrieval the structural signal collapses toward uniformity, diagnosing a regime boundary where reasoning-level consistency evaluation is uninformative. The two components relate differently to accuracy: within-trial ambiguity correlates positively with correctness -- consistent with settings where multiple plausible solution paths remain competitive -- while across-trial instability correlates negatively, signaling unreliable reasoning. Structural uncertainty is best understood not as a universal confidence estimator, but as a regime-sensitive evaluator of logical reasoning consistency.

</details>


### [148] [MemTrace: Probing What Final Accuracy Misses in Long-Term Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17328)
*Xianxuan Long,Zhikai Chen,Shenglai Zeng,Shouren Wang,Kai Guo,Jiliang Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MemTrace 是一个以知识点为单位评估大语言模型代理长期记忆的基准，通过控制记忆年龄、问题类型和证据条件三个维度，揭示了现有方法在评估记忆性能时的局限性。研究发现，尽管整体准确率相似，但不同系统在处理事实变化、应对错误前提等方面表现差异显著，且失败的主要原因是证据利用不足而非检索困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对 LLM 代理长期记忆的评估方式仅基于问题行的独立准确率，无法反映同一事实在不同情境下的行为变化，导致隐藏了关键缺陷。因此需要一种更精细的评估框架来揭示记忆系统的真正能力与瓶颈。

Method: 提出 MemTrace 基准，将评估单位从单个问题改为知识点（单一用户事实），并系统地在记忆年龄、问题类型（当前状态、历史状态、变化轨迹）和证据条件（存在、缺失、矛盾前提）三个维度上进行测试，评估13种记忆配置在四种范式下的表现。

Result: 不同配置在总准确率上相似，但行为差异显著：恢复当前或历史状态并不等于能追踪变化；安全回避也不代表能纠正错误前提。主要瓶颈在于证据使用，而非检索——失败时证据可被检索的概率是缺失的10倍。

Conclusion: 提升长期记忆的关键不在于增加存储或改进检索，而在于优化对已获取证据的有效利用。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly maintain long-term memory of user facts across sessions. Yet such memory is usually evaluated by aggregating accuracy over question rows or episodes. Because this approach scores question rows independently, even when several questions probe the same fact, it cannot show how that fact behaves as conditions change. We introduce MemTrace, a benchmark whose unit of measurement is the knowledge point: a single typed fact about the user, rather than an individual question. MemTrace probes each fact along three controlled dimensions: memory age, defined by how many sessions ago the fact appeared in the history; question type, covering current state, earlier state, and trajectory of change; and evidence condition, covering present, missing, and contradicted-by-false-premise settings. Evaluating 13 memory-system configurations across four paradigms, we find that similar pooled accuracy hides different failures: recovering a fact's current and earlier states does not imply tracking how it changed, and safe abstention does not imply correcting a false premise. The dominant bottleneck is evidence use, not retrieval: when systems fail, the evidence was retrievable 10 times more often than it was missing. These results suggest that improving long-term memory requires better use of reachable evidence, not simply more storage or retrieval.

</details>


### [149] [SpeechDx: A Multi-Task Benchmark for Clinical Speech AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17339)
*Sejal Bhalla,Larry Kieu,Aina Merchant,Eyal de Lara,Alex Mariakakis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SpeechDx 是一个大规模临床语音人工智能基准，涵盖12个数据集和27个任务，覆盖多种健康状况。它通过语音生成阶段（概念化、构想、发音）结构化任务，评估模型在有限标注数据和跨数据集条件下的泛化能力，以区分临床有意义的模式与数据集伪影。系统评估了12个最先进的音频编码器，并测试了零样本跨条件迁移。结果表明，大规模语音模型是最佳基线，领域特定模型仅在任务匹配时表现更好，当前表示无法可靠地跨临床语音场景泛化。SpeechDx 建立了一个共享评估框架，用于追踪通用临床语音表示的发展进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有临床语音AI研究多为孤立的特定疾病研究，导致结果难以比较，泛化能力难以评估。需要一个统一的基准来推动通用临床语音表示的发展。

Method: 构建SpeechDx基准，包含12个数据集和27个任务，按语音生成阶段（概念化、构想、发音）分类；评估模型在少标签数据和跨数据集条件下的表现，进行零样本跨条件迁移测试；系统评估12种先进音频编码器。

Result: 大规模语音模型表现最优，领域特定模型仅在任务相近时提升性能，无现有表示能可靠跨不同临床条件泛化。

Conclusion: SpeechDx 提供了一个共享评估框架，有助于推动通用临床语音表示的研究与进展。

Abstract: Speech offers a uniquely informative window into health by simultaneously engaging neurological, motor, respiratory, and vocal systems. Current clinical speech AI methods have largely progressed through isolated condition-specific studies, making results difficult to compare and generalization difficult to assess. We introduce SpeechDx, a large-scale benchmark for clinical speech AI spanning 12 datasets and 27 tasks across diverse health conditions. To enable evaluation across shared clinical mechanisms, SpeechDx structures tasks by the stage of speech production they disrupt: conceptualization, formulation, and articulation. The benchmark tests generalization by including tasks with limited labeled data and evaluating the same health condition across multiple datasets, distinguishing clinically meaningful patterns from dataset artefacts. We systematically evaluate 12 state-of-the-art audio encoders across all tasks and under zero-shot cross-condition transfer. Results show that large-scale speech models represent the strongest overall baselines, domain-specific models improve performance only on closely matched tasks, and no current representation generalizes reliably across the clinical speech landscape. SpeechDx establishes a shared evaluation framework for tracking progress toward general-purpose clinical speech representations

### [150] [Distributed General-Purpose Agent Networks: Architecture, Key Mechanisms, and Prototypes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17368)

Abstract: Large language models have accelerated the transition from passive conversational assistants to autonomous agents that can understand goals, plan actions, invoke tools, and execute multi-step tasks. Yet the capability of a single agent remains constrained by its local data, tool permissions, runtime environment, and governance boundary. This paper studies distributed general-purpose agent networks: open peer-to-peer networks in which heterogeneous agents deployed on personal devices, edge nodes, or autonomous computing environments can discover one another, establish trust, negotiate cooperation rules, and execute open-ended tasks. We argue that such networks cannot be obtained by simply combining existing peer-to-peer overlays with conventional multi-agent systems. Unlike traditional P2P networks, agent networks must propagate semantic declarations about intentions, capabilities, states, and cooperation constraints. We therefore propose a layered architecture centered on a protocol adaptation layer that connects upper-level task semantics with lower-level network operations. Based on this architecture, the paper identifies three core mechanism problems: semantic announcement propagation for collaborator discovery, verifiable identity and multi-topic reputation for cooperation governance, and semantic-gradient mechanism design for open task execution. For each problem, we present a technical route, including bodyless gossip with sequential logs, BAID-based identity binding with MG-EigenTrust reputation, and a Stackelberg-style mechanism-generation loop driven by semantic attribution feedback. We further report prototype overhead results for BAID-style tiered verification and mechanism-level simulations of MG-EigenTrust under cross-topic disguise-collusion attacks. The resulting framework provides a system-level foundation for open, trustworthy, and scalable agent collaboration.

The AI system is initially trained on historical medical records and operates in a continuous learning loop. ### [152] [Incumbent Advantage: Brand Bias and Cognitive Manipulation Dynamics in LLM Recommendation Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17443)
*Xi Chu,Yupeng Hou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在护肤品推荐中的品牌竞争动态，发现知名品牌在相同规格下几乎100%被推荐（条件垄断），但微小的评分优势即可打破这一垄断；使用权威式营销语言（如虚构临床证据）可带来额外0.17分的评分优势，且各模型反应不同；在多品牌竞争中，若所有品牌采用相同优化策略，个体收益大幅下降，非参与者则完全得不到推荐。研究指出生成式引擎优化（GEO）不仅是安全风险，更是一种正在塑造市场竞争的新营销实践。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过三个实验，研究在三种商业级LLM（GPT-4o-mini、Claude Sonnet、Gemini 3 Flash）上对护肤品进行推荐行为分析，控制产品规格一致性的条件下测试品牌知名度的影响，并引入营销语言和评分差异变量，同时设置搜索商品作为稳健性检验。

Conclusion: 生成式引擎优化（GEO）不仅构成潜在安全风险，更正演变为一种新兴的市场营销实践，深刻影响市场结构与竞争格局，应受到学术界与产业界的共同关注。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are becoming a major way for consumers to find products, but we do not yet understand how brands compete in this new channel. We study brand dynamics in LLM recommendations using skincare products -- a category where consumers cannot easily judge quality before buying and must rely on brand reputation -- across three commercial LLMs (GPT-4o-mini, Claude Sonnet, Gemini 3 Flash), with a robustness check on search goods. In three experiments, we find: (1) a Conditional Monopoly where well-known brands get recommended 100% of the time (IAI = 10.0) when all products have the same specifications, but this dominance disappears with less than a +0.1-star rating advantage for a competitor; (2) authority-style marketing language, including fabricated clinical-evidence claims, breaks this monopoly at a Bias Surplus Value equal to +0.17 rating points, with each model responding differently; and (3) a social dilemma in multi-brand GEO competition: when all brands adopt the same optimization strategy, individual payoff falls from +0.802 to +0.007 in our payoff proxy, and non-participating brands receive zero recommendations in our tests. Our results suggest that generative engine optimization (GEO) should be studied not only as a security risk, but also as an emerging marketing practice that shapes market competition.

We propose a Machine-Learned Comorbidity Index (MLCI) that maps diagnosis codes to a single scalar by maximizing the normalized Hilbert-Schmidt Independence Criterion (nHSIC) between the learned score and multiple clinical outcomes. MLCI captures nonlinear risk-outcome dependence and is supported by a theory that characterizes when a unified, informative admission-level ordering can be achieved across outcomes. ### [154] [MapSatisfyBench: Benchmarking Satisfaction-Aware Map Agents through Behavior-Grounded Implicit Decision Factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17453)
*Lubin Bai,Mengyu Cao,Sixue Wang,Zhongwei Wan,Yue Pan,Jiale Hou,Xiang Li,Xiuyuan Zhang*

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种restore-identify-filter框架，通过行为链证据重建用户完整需求，识别并保留可由查询前信息支持的隐式决策因素。基于此，构建了MapSatisfyBench基准，利用真实世界匿名数据从五个维度标注真实答案，实现对满意度感知地图智能体的全流程评估。实验表明，现有智能体在显式任务完成上表现良好，但在满足隐式决策因素及主动获取满意度相关证据方面仍受限。该工作推动地图智能体评估从任务完成转向满意度感知的空间决策。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出restore-identify-filter框架：首先重构用户行为链以恢复完整需求；其次识别潜在隐式决策因素；最后筛选仅由预查询证据支持的因素。基于该方法，构建MapSatisfyBench基准，利用大规模真实用户数据，从五个维度标注真实标签，支持端到端的满意度感知评估。

Result: 实验显示，当前地图智能体在显式任务完成方面表现良好，但在满足隐式决策因素和主动获取满意度相关证据方面能力有限。MapSatisfyBench有效支撑了从任务完成向满意度感知空间决策的评估范式转变。

Conclusion: MapSatisfyBench为地图智能体评估提供了新基准，推动评估重点从任务完成转向满意度感知的空间决策，揭示了现有智能体在处理隐式需求方面的不足，为未来研究指明方向。

Abstract: Large language model agents are increasingly integrated into map services. Since map services are embedded in everyday-life scenarios rather than professional task settings, users often express their needs informally, resulting in underspecified queries with many unspoken needs, namely, implicit decision factors that are critical for user satisfaction. Although clarification is an effective way to mitigate this issue, it increases user burden in daily interaction, and a capable agent should first proactively recover such factors from available information sources. However, evaluating this ability is challenging. The first challenge is to determine which implicit decision factors are suitable for evaluation. A factor is evaluable only if it affects user acceptance and can be recovered from information available to the agent before it responds. Second, user satisfaction cannot be reliably represented by a single reference answer, requiring a benchmark that converts satisfaction-relevant factors into objective and quantifiable evaluation targets. To address these challenges, we propose a restore-identify-filter framework that reconstructs complete user needs from behavior-chain evidence, identifies implicit decision factors, and retains only those supported by pre-query evidence. Building on this methodology, we construct MapSatisfyBench from large-scale, real-world anonymized user data and annotate ground truth from five dimensions and enables full-chain evaluation of satisfaction-aware map agents. Experiments show that current agents generally perform well on explicit task completion, but remain limited in satisfying implicit decision factors and proactively acquiring the evidence needed for satisfaction-aware decisions. These findings establish MapSatisfyBench as a benchmark for shifting map-agent evaluation from task completion toward satisfaction-aware spatial decision making.

### [155] [Dissecting model behavior through agent trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17454)
*Gaurav Gupta,Vatshank Chaturvedi,Jun Huan,Anoop Deoras*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出‘意图-执行’差距是影响AI代理性能的核心系统问题，强调模型与执行框架之间的对齐至关重要。通过构建可定制的简单代理框架SSA，作者在多个基准测试中复现或超越了现有模型表现，并基于13.8万条轨迹分析揭示了不同模型在问题解决过程中的行为差异，如编辑频率、测试活动和阶段转换等细粒度行为特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代理性能不仅取决于模型能力，更受其执行框架（harness）的影响。模型意图与实际执行之间存在差距，这种‘意图-执行’不一致会限制模型潜力的发挥，因此需要重视框架设计与模型之间的对齐。

Method: 提出Simple Strands Agent (SSA) 框架，用于捕捉跨模型家族的通用行为模式，并识别少量模型特异性偏好；利用大规模轨迹数据（138k条）在代码状态空间中分析代理行为，引入编辑频率、测试活动、阶段转换等细粒度指标来刻画模型的问题求解策略差异。

Result: SSA在SWE-Pro、SWE-Verified和Terminal-Bench-2等基准上复现或提升了各模型提供商报告的pass@1性能；通过细粒度分析发现不同模型在问题解决过程中存在显著的行为差异，揭示了模型如何分配精力于不同阶段。

Conclusion: 最小化‘意图-执行’差距是提升AI代理性能的关键，不应仅关注模型本身或工具集成，而应将框架设计与模型行为对齐视为同等重要。细粒度轨迹分析为理解模型行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: AI agent performance is not just a modeling problem, it is fundamentally a systems problem. The advanced capabilities of models are realized through agent harnesses. Therefore, a gap between model assumptions and harness behavior can easily prevent the model's full capabilities from translating into agent performance. We formalize this as the `intent-execution' gap: the mismatch between what the model intends and what the harness executes, and vice versa. We argue that minimizing this intent-execution gap is as important as other aspects of harness design such as tools and execution loops. To illustrate the impact of this harness-model alignment, we develop a simple and customizable harness called `Simple Strands Agent' (SSA). SSA aims to find the bulk of common patterns which generalize across different model families (such as Claude, Gemini, GPT, Grok, Qwen), as well as a small number of model-specific preferences. We make two contributions: (i) we $\textbf{reproduce or improve on the pass@1}$ performance reported by diverse model-provider families on popular agentic benchmarks (SWE-Pro, SWE-Verified and Terminal-Bench-2), and (ii) building on an $\textbf{analysis of 138k trajectories generated by SSA}$, we look beyond the $\texttt{pass@1}$ numbers which tend to be relatively even across frontier models. By representing agent trajectories in code state-spaces, we observe model-level differences in problem-solving behavior. Finer-grained metrics such as edit frequency, testing activity, and phase-transitions reveal how individual models allocate effort across different stages of autonomous problem solving.

</details>


### [156] [Can LLMs Be CEOs? Benchmarking Strategic Resource Reallocation with Multi-Role Agent Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17459)
*Yuyang Dai,Xueqing Peng,Lingfei Qian,Zhuohan Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 	extsc{CEO-Bench}，一个用于评估大语言模型在模拟首席执行官战略资源再分配决策能力的多智能体基准。该基准模拟真实企业环境中信息不对称、角色冲突与时间依赖等挑战，要求模型整合来自四位具有私有信息和不同目标的高管（CFO、CTO、COO、CMO）的矛盾建议，并生成符合四维评估标准（角色整合、条件胆略、历史敏感性、计划有效性）的决策方案。实验发现所有模型在结构有效性上表现良好，但在战略校准方面差异显著，存在单方影响捕获、模糊情境下的保守倾向及历史遗忘等系统性失败模式，并揭示了深度整合与决策果断性之间的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型评估主要聚焦于孤立的认知任务，如推理、知识检索和经济理性，但忽略了真实企业决策中面临的复杂性：即在信息不对称、组织约束和时间依赖背景下，如何整合来自多个专业利益相关者的矛盾建议。因此亟需更贴近真实管理场景的评估框架。

Method: 构建一个多智能体环境，其中大语言模型作为CEO，接收四位角色特化的高管（CFO、CTO、COO、CMO）提供的带有私有信号和不同优先级的建议；模型需综合这些信息，在多轮互动中制定资源分配计划，并依据四个维度进行评估：角色整合度、条件胆略性、历史敏感性与计划有效性。

Result: 所有前沿模型在计划结构有效性上表现良好，但在战略校准能力上差距明显。识别出三类系统性失败模式：单一顾问主导、模糊情境下的保守默认、以及对历史信息的忽视。进一步发现，模型越深入整合多方意见，其决策越缺乏决断力，形成‘整合-胆略’权衡。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在模拟高层管理者决策时仍处于初级阶段，虽能处理结构化任务，但难以实现真正的战略协调与动态权衡。该研究为未来人机协同决策系统的设计提供了关键洞见与技术边界。

Abstract: Evaluating the decision-making capabilities of large language models (LLMs) is a growing research priority, yet existing benchmarks focus on isolated cognitive tasks such as reasoning, knowledge retrieval, and economic rationality in stylized settings. These evaluations overlook the defining challenge of real executive decision-making: integrating conflicting recommendations from specialized stakeholders under information asymmetry, organizational constraints, and temporal dependencies. We introduce \textsc{CEO-Bench}, a multi-agent benchmark that evaluates LLMs on CEO-level strategic resource reallocation -- the process of redirecting capital across business units in a multi-round, constraint-rich organizational environment. In \textsc{CEO-Bench}, LLM agents receive conflicting advice from four role-conditioned C-suite advisors (CFO, CTO, COO, CMO), each with private signals and distinct priorities, and must synthesize these into a concrete allocation plan evaluated along four dimensions: role integration, conditional boldness, history-sensitive judgment, and plan validity. Experiments across five frontier models on 13 scenarios reveal that all models achieve high structural validity but diverge sharply on strategic calibration -- the hardest capability layer. We identify systematic failure modes including single-advisor capture, conservative default under ambiguity, and historical amnesia, and uncover a structural integration-boldness tradeoff: models that engage more deeply with conflicting perspectives tend to produce less decisive action. These findings delineate the current capability boundary of LLMs as organizational decision-makers and inform the design of future AI-assisted executive systems.

Preliminary evaluation shows that the proposed LLM-as-Judge pipeline delivers marking outcomes comparable to human tutors, while yielding justifications that are more traceable to authorised curriculum artefacts and marking standards. ### [158] [SEAGym: An Evaluation Environment for Self-Evolving LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17546)
*Congjie Zheng,Chuanyi Xue,Bin Liang,Jun Yang,Changshui Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出SEAGym，一个用于评估基于大语言模型的自演化代理在代理框架更新方面的动态评估环境。该框架通过训练、验证、测试、回放和成本记录等多维度评估代理改进是否具有可复用性、是否过拟合近期任务、是否增加成本或损害旧行为。在Terminal-Bench 2.0和HLE上的实验表明，不同评估视角提供互补信号，揭示频繁更新未必提升泛化性能，中间有效快照可能后期失效，且源数据多样性和模型后端会影响框架可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对自演化代理的评估通常仅依赖单一任务得分或顺序曲线，无法全面反映更新是否带来可复用改进、是否存在过拟合、成本变化或对旧行为的负面影响，亟需更系统、动态的评估机制。

Method: 提出SEAGym评估环境，将Harbor兼容基准转化为动态自演化任务源，支持训练批次、冻结更新-验证、内部与外部数据分布转移视图、回放诊断以及快照和指标记录，实现多阶段、多维度评估。

Result: 在Terminal-Bench 2.0和HLE上对比ACE、TF-GRPO和AHE方法发现：不同评估视图揭示了互补信息——频繁更新未必提升泛化表现，有用中间快照可能后期崩溃，源数据多样性与模型后端显著影响代理框架的稳定性与可靠性。

Conclusion: SEAGym为自演化代理框架的改进提供了全面、动态的评估能力，能够揭示传统评估忽略的关键问题，有助于开发更稳健、可持续演化的智能代理系统。

Abstract: Self-evolving LLM-based agents improve mainly by changing their agent harness: the structured execution layer around a base model, including prompts, memory, tools, middleware, runtime state, and the model-tool interaction loop. Existing evaluations often reduce this process to isolated task scores or a single sequential curve, obscuring whether an update produces reusable improvement, overfits recent tasks, increases cost, or harms older behavior. We introduce SEAGym, an evaluation environment for measuring agent harness updates across training, validation, test, replay, and cost records. SEAGym turns Harbor-compatible benchmarks into dynamic self-evolution task sources with train batches, frozen update-validation, held-out ID and OOD transfer views, replay diagnostics, and saved snapshot and metric records. Instantiating SEAGym on Terminal-Bench 2.0 and HLE, we compare ACE, TF-GRPO, and AHE under a shared epoch/batch protocol. The results show that these evaluation views provide complementary signals about the evolution process: frequent updates may fail to improve held-out performance, useful intermediate snapshots may collapse later, and source diversity and model backend can affect harness reliability.

### [159] [DeepInsight: A Unified Evaluation Infrastructure Across the Physical AI Stack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17574)
*Siyi Li,Chunyu Sun,Jiahao Zhang,Yuchen Kang,Wuliang Wang,Yu Qiu,Rui Jiang,Haitao Cui,Jie Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DeepInsight 是一个统一的评估基础设施，能够跨越从单个基础模型解码到数千次物理模拟步长的多量级操作，通过三个核心抽象（任务、资源、结果）实现全栈一致性评估。它在保持各层异质性的同时，提供共享的运行时和追踪机制，使跨层问题可定位，显著提升诊断效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架无法覆盖从基础模型推理到全身控制等多量级操作的完整物理AI栈评估需求，导致各模块评估独立、缺乏统一追踪，难以诊断跨层回归问题。

Method: 提出DeepInsight，通过统一的episode驱动器、资源句柄协议和追踪身份方案，构建单一运行时环境，支持多层级系统评估，并保留各层特性。

Result: 在生产环境中部署于具身人形机器人栈的三层，新基准可通过配置快速接入；在基础模型层面复现已有基准结果，运行更快且具备近线性扩展能力；关键优势在于跨层问题可追溯至同一追踪日志，实现精准诊断。

Conclusion: DeepInsight 通过共享不变量实现了对复杂物理AI栈的统一评估，解决了跨层调试难题，是现有分段评估框架无法比拟的系统级进步。

Abstract: Evaluating a Physical AI stack spans operators that differ by more than three orders of magnitude -- from a single foundation-model decoding step to thousands of physics ticks of whole-body control -- varying orthogonally in modality, reward semantics, and resource profile. No existing framework spans this range, so the stack is evaluated today by stitching together separate harnesses that share neither runtime nor scoring, preserving each segment's local validity but losing the shared identity needed to diagnose cross-layer regressions. We present DeepInsight, an evaluation infrastructure that serves this full spectrum on a single runtime. Rather than homogenize the regimes, it preserves their heterogeneity behind three narrow abstractions -- task, resource, and result -- each realized as one invariant shared by every subsystem: one episode driver, one resource-handle protocol implemented by every expensive backend (LLM inference and sandboxed runtimes alike), and one trace identity scheme under which every event is written. Deployed in production across all three layers of an embodied humanoid stack, this single set of invariants onboards new benchmarks largely by configuration. Where mature peer orchestrators exist -- at the foundation-model end -- it reproduces published references and peer-framework readings within their own spread, runs the same suites faster on a single node, and scales near-linearly across nodes. Its distinctive return is diagnostic: because every layer writes into one shared trace, a regression that begins in one layer and surfaces in another stays localizable on that trace -- a cross-layer payoff no federation of per-segment harnesses can reproduce.

</details>

Abstract: AI-driven engineering workflows face particular challenges in crash safety design: unlike aerodynamics, crash events involve highly nonlinear contact dynamics, material nonlinearity, and discrete state transitions that are difficult to capture with data-driven surrogate models. To the best of our knowledge, we present the first foundation model--orchestrated workflow for crash safety design that enables surrogate-assisted exploration for pedestrian protection, reducing evaluation time from hours per CAE simulation to seconds.
  The workflow integrates four components: (1) a surrogate trained on CAE crash simulations to predict pedestrian leg injury metrics from design parameters, achieving an average $R^2=0.87$ and providing distribution-free conformal prediction intervals; (2) multiobjective evolutionary search (NSGA-II) to discover diverse feasible parameter sets under user-specified constraints; (3) a morphing-based geometry generator that maps parameters to topology-preserving 3D shapes; and (4) a natural-language interface in which an LLM orchestrates the workflow and a vision--language model supports semantic comparison of generated designs.
  In an automotive front-bumper case study, the workflow produces 35 distinct safety-compliant alternatives from a single exploration, a process that would require weeks with conventional CAE iteration. These results suggest that foundation models can serve as integration layers between ML surrogates and physics-based simulation, helping bring AI capabilities to safety-critical engineering domains.

### [161] [Closing the Feedback Loop: From Experience Extraction to Insight Governance in Verbal Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17591)
*Yanwei Cui,Xing Zhang,Yulong Zhang,Li Shao,Xiaofeng Shi,Guanghui Wang,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种无需训练的语义强化学习方法，通过从世界反馈中提取语义规则并注入上下文来更新大语言模型（LLM）代理的行为，而无需修改参数。在非平稳环境中，传统方法面临保留过时知识与遗忘重要经验之间的困境。作者识别出四个关键需求：基于结果的评估、持续的结构化证据、非单调的知识生命周期和组合式治理，并指出现有方法过度关注经验提取而忽视洞察治理。为此，提出一个三层架构（规则、证据、技能），通过反馈驱动的优化循环实现闭环治理。在金融预测案例中，有无该机制导致性能从低于零样本基线到显著提升的差异，验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平稳环境中，现有训练-free强化学习方法因无法有效管理过时或错误的经验，导致负迁移或灾难性遗忘，亟需一种机制来平衡经验的保留与淘汰，实现长期适应能力。

Method: 提出三层次架构：规则层（从世界反馈中提炼经验）、证据层（记录每条规则在不同情境下的可靠性）、技能层（决定何时应用规则、如何解决冲突、是否回避决策）。通过反馈驱动的持续优化循环，实现对知识的动态治理。

Result: 在金融预测任务中，仅依赖经验提取的方法使模型性能下降至低于零样本基线；而引入所提出的治理机制后，模型准确率和风险调整后收益显著提升，证明了该框架的有效性与必要性。

Conclusion: 有效的知识治理是实现训练-free强化学习在非平稳环境长期稳定表现的关键。本研究所提的三层次架构与反馈驱动的治理循环，能够有效缓解保留-遗忘困境，为大模型智能体的自适应演化提供新范式。

Abstract: Training-free verbal reinforcement learning enables LLM agents to learn from world feedback -- objective signals such as dynamic task outcomes, market returns, or demand forecasts -- by extracting verbal rules from experience and injecting them as context, updating the agent's behavior without parameter changes. However, in non-stationary environments these agents face a retention-forgetting dilemma: retaining stale insights causes negative transfer, while discarding them causes catastrophic forgetting when conditions recur. We identify four requirements for navigating this dilemma -- outcome-driven evaluation, persistent structured evidence, non-monotonic knowledge lifecycle, and compositional governance -- and show that existing methods invest heavily in experience extraction while underinvesting in insight governance. We propose a three-layer architecture -- rules, evidence, and skills -- connected by a feedback-driven curation loop that closes the governance gap. Rules capture distilled experience from world outcomes; evidence logs track each rule's reliability across episodes; skills govern which rules to apply, how to resolve conflicts, and when to abstain. On financial forecasting as a case study, where world feedback is naturally abundant, noisy, and non-stationary, we show that the same accumulated experience either degrades performance below the zero-shot baseline or dramatically improves accuracy and risk-adjusted returns, depending on whether the curation loop is present.

### [162] [Brick-DICL: Dynamic In-Context Learning for Automated Brick Schema Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17637)
*Yiyue Qian,Shinan Zhang,Huan Song,Negin Sokhandan,Hannah Marlowe,Diego Socolinsky*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Brick-DICL，一种两阶段动态上下文学习框架，用于自动化建筑信息模型（Brick）模式分类。该框架通过元数据-RAG和类别-RAG增强大语言模型的领域知识并缩小分类空间，结合多大语言模型过滤机制，显著提升分类准确率并减少人工验证工作量，适用于不同厂商和格式的楼宇管理系统，推动标准化、互操作性楼宇管理系统的实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有楼宇管理系统（BMS）因制造商间缺乏标准化，导致数据整合与利用困难；尽管Brick模式提供标准化本体，但其庞大的类数量（936个）、大语言模型领域知识有限以及手动验证成本高，限制了实际应用。因此亟需一种高效、准确且通用的自动化映射方法。

Method: 提出Brick-DICL框架，包含两个阶段：(1) metadata-RAG从相关示例中检索信息以增强LLM的领域理解；(2) class-RAG缩小潜在的Brick类范围以应对大规模分类空间。同时引入多LLM过滤机制，比较多个模型预测结果，对低置信度分类进行标记供人工审核。

Result: Brick-DICL在多个建筑数据集上表现出色，显著提升分类准确性，优于现有方法；有效降低人工验证需求，加速数字楼宇上线过程；具备跨厂商、跨格式的通用性，推动建筑系统标准化与互操作性发展。

Conclusion: Brick-DICL是首个针对Brick模式分类的动态上下文学习框架，兼具通用性、高效性和高精度，为构建标准化、可扩展的智能建筑管理系统提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: Building Management Systems (BMS) are essential for optimizing energy efficiency and operational performance in modern buildings. However, the lack of standardization across BMS points from different manufacturers creates significant barriers to integration and data utilization. While the Brick schema offers a standardized ontology for building systems, mapping BMS points to appropriate Brick classes presents three critical challenges: (i) the extensive number of Brick classes (936 in the latest version), (ii) limited domain-specific knowledge in large language models (LLMs), and (iii) substantial manual effort required for verification. To address these challenges, we propose Brick-DICL, a two-stage dynamic in-context learning framework for automated Brick schema classification. Brick-DICL consists of two primary components: metadata-RAG, which retrieves relevant examples to enhance LLMs' domain knowledge, and class-RAG, which narrows down potential Brick classes to address the large classification space. Additionally, we implement a multi-LLM filtering mechanism that compares predictions across multiple models, flagging low-confidence classifications for human review. As a result: (i) General: Brick-DICL is applicable to any building management system regardless of manufacturer or metadata format; (ii) Novel and Powerful: as the first dynamic in-context learning approach for Brick schema classification, Brick-DICL achieves significant classification accuracy improvements on building datasets, outperforming existing methods; (iii) Efficient: our multi-LLM filtering strategy reduces manual verification effort, enabling rapid digital building onboarding. Extensive experiments demonstrate Brick-DICL's effectiveness across diverse building datasets, accelerating the path toward standardized, interoperable building management systems.

### [163] [FinAcumen: Financial Multimodal Reasoning via Self-Evolving Experience Memory Harness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17642)
*Pianran Guo,Pengcheng Zhou,Yucheng Jian,Shuhua Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FinAcumen 是一个专注于金融多模态推理的智能体框架，通过选择性经验记忆机制，使智能体在跨任务中积累并复用成功的推理策略和失败警示规则，从而提升推理可靠性。该框架通过语义相关性阈值控制经验激活，并结合确定性金融工具环境，有效减少噪声检索与幻觉推理，在多个金融多模态基准上超越了冻结的8B视觉语言模型及专业金融模型，接近领先通用模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具增强型智能体在金融多模态推理中缺乏跨会话的状态记忆，导致重复发现错误模式、工具路由不可靠、检索噪声大且推理易产生幻觉，尤其在高风险金融场景下表现不稳定。因此亟需一种能持续积累经验并智能调用的推理框架。

Method: 提出 FinAcumen 框架，构建持久化经验记忆库，从过往推理轨迹中提炼成功策略与失败警示规则；推理时仅当经验与当前任务语义相关性超过预设阈值时才激活，否则通过回退机制抑制无关记忆；结合确定性金融工具环境实现数值计算、信息检索、视觉解码与答案验证的精准对齐。

Result: 在四个金融多模态推理基准测试中，FinAcumen 显著优于冻结的8B视觉语言模型及专门训练的金融模型，性能接近领先商用通用模型；实验表明，在检索不确定性环境下，选择性经验激活显著提升了推理稳定性与可靠性。

Conclusion: FinAcumen 通过选择性经验记忆机制实现了金融多模态推理中长期知识积累与可靠决策，为高精度、低风险金融智能系统提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Financial multimodal reasoning requires agents to coordinate numerical computation, retrieval, visual interpretation, and temporal grounding across heterogeneous evidence sources. Existing tool-augmented agents improve execution fidelity, yet remain largely stateless across episodes, repeatedly rediscovering reasoning strategies and failure patterns. In high-stakes financial settings, this leads to unreliable tool routing, noisy retrieval, and hallucination-prone reasoning. We present FinAcumen, a financial reasoning agent framework centered on selective experience memory for tool-augmented multimodal reasoning. FinAcumen accumulates financially grounded reasoning experience from prior trajectories, distilling successful strategies and failure-derived cautionary rules into a persistent memory bank. During inference, retrieved experiences condition reasoning only when semantic relevance exceeds a calibrated threshold, while irrelevant memory is explicitly suppressed through a fallback mechanism. A deterministic financial tool environment further grounds numerical computation, retrieval, visual decoding, and answer verification.Across four financial multimodal reasoning benchmarks, FinAcumen consistently improves a frozen 8B vision-language model over finance-specialized models and approaches leading proprietary general-purpose models. Further analysis shows that selective experience activation improves reasoning reliability under retrieval uncertainty. Our code is anonymously available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/FinAcumen

### [164] [Beyond Domains: Reusing Web Skills via Transferable Interaction Patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17645)
*Shiqi He,Yue Cui,Feijie Wu,Xinyu Ma,Jiaheng Lu,Yaliang Li,Bolin Ding,Mosharaf Chowdhury*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillMigrator 是一种新型网页智能体，通过基于布局结构匹配而非具体元素引用来迁移和复用网页技能，从而减少LLM调用次数。它将每个技能存储为可迁移的交互模式（TIP），包含技能与诱导时的结构草图。测试时，通过布局相似性检索TIP，并在实时页面上定位其引用。相比现有方法，在保持成功率的前提下，显著降低了平均LLM动作数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网页技能库主要依赖指令相似性或粗粒度站点元数据进行触发，导致跨站点技能复用率低，无法充分实现步骤与令牌的压缩。因此需要更有效的技能迁移机制以提升效率。

Method: 提出SkillMigrator系统，利用布局结构相似性匹配技能，将每个技能与其诱导时刻的结构草图结合形成可迁移的交互模式（TIP）。测试时根据当前页面布局相似性检索并接地于实际页面，结合标准的无障碍快照观测与工具调用流程。

Result: 在WebArena和Mind2Web基准上，相较于最先进方法，SkillMigrator在相同成功率下将平均LLM动作数减少了8-10%。

Conclusion: 通过基于布局结构的技能迁移，SkillMigrator有效提升了网页技能的跨站点复用能力，显著降低推理过程中的模型调用开销，是高效网页智能体的重要进展。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) web agents are usually deployed as tool callers: each turn, the model reads a fresh page observation and emits one structured tool action. When every action is a low-level primitive, horizons grow quickly and so do policy-facing LLM completions, dominating latency and cost on benchmarks such as Mind2Web and WebArena. Recent systems therefore wrap repeated interaction fragments as web skills: callable tools built from successful trajectories or induced programs, so one call can replace several primitives. However, prior skill libraries are still triggered mainly by instruction similarity or coarse site metadata, which yields low skill reuse on held-out sites and leaves much of the potential step and token reduction on the table.
  We present SkillMigrator, an agent that learns reusable web skills and transfers them across sites by matching layout structure rather than specific element references. Each induced skill is stored as a transferable interaction pattern (TIP): the skill paired with a structural sketch of the snapshot at induction time. At test time, SkillMigrator retrieves TIPs by layout similarity and grounds their references on the live page. The rest of the stack is standard: accessibility-snapshot observations with stable references, and fixed tool calling over primitives plus skill invocations. Compared with the state-of-the-art approaches, SkillMigrator reduces the average LLM-action count on successful trajectories by 8-10% across both WebArena and Mind2Web at matched success rate.

### [165] [From Brewing to Resolution: Tracing the Internal Lifecycle of Code Reasoning in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17648)
*Siyue Chen,Yifu Guo,Yuquan Lu,Zishan Xu,Jiaye Lin,Jianbo Lin,Siyu Zhang,Cheng Yang,Junxin Li,Yujia Li,Yu Huo,Ruixuan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大语言模型在代码推理中的内部生命周期，提出‘酿造’（brewing）现象——模型在早期层中已生成答案线索，但需多层后才可自解。通过双诊断框架（层间线性探测与上下文剥离解码），发现四种结果：已解决、过度处理、错误解决、未解决，其中仅41.5%任务被正确解决。不同架构和规模下‘酿造’阶段稳定存在（24-42%），而解决成功率随能力、规模和训练变化，表明酿造是通用规律，而解决能力则因模型差异而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准准确率无法解释为何LLMs能处理变量追踪却失败于语义等价循环，需要深入理解其内部推理过程的动态机制。

Method: 引入双诊断框架，结合层间线性探测与上下文剥离解码（CSD），分析16个模型在六类代码推理任务中的内部行为。

Result: 所有任务中四种结果均有显著分布；整体解决率仅41.5%，部分任务低于30%；函数调用深度增加导致解决率从61.1%降至2.5%；酿造阶段持续稳定（24-42%），分辨率成功与模型能力正相关。

Conclusion: ‘酿造’是decoder-only Transformer模型中一种稳定的内在规律，而最终解决能力取决于模型规模、训练质量与能力水平，提示需超越表面准确率进行深层评估。

Abstract: Standard accuracy metrics cannot explain why LLMs handle variable tracking but fail on semantically equivalent loops. We study an internal lifecycle of code reasoning in which models first brew the answer, making it linearly recoverable many layers before it becomes self-decodable, and then diverge into one of four resolution outcomes: Resolved, Overprocessed, Misresolved, or Unresolved. Understanding this lifecycle matters because similar task accuracies can mask fundamentally different failure modes that surface-level evaluation cannot detect. We introduce a dual diagnostic framework pairing layer-wise linear probing with Context-Stripped Decoding (CSD) and apply it to six code-reasoning task families across 16 models spanning Qwen, Llama, and DeepSeek architectures. All four outcomes carry substantial mass in every task family: overall Resolved is only 41.5%, with multiple tasks below 30%. Controlled sweeps over structure, depth, and operators expose task-specific failure bottlenecks: Function Call Resolved plunges from 61.1% to 2.5% as call depth increases from one to three. Across architectures and scales, the brewing scaffold remains stable, with normalized brewing duration 24-42% across all 16 models, while resolution success varies with capability. This indicates that the scaffold is a stable empirical regularity across the tested decoder-only Transformer families, whereas resolution success covaries with capability, scale, and training. Code: https://github.com/euyis1019/llm-brewing

</details>


### [166] [Using Cognitive Models to Improve Language Model Simulation of Human Persuasion Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17657)
*Zirui Cheng,Zeyu Shen,Thomas L. Griffiths,Peter Henderson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为Equation-to-Behavior Prompting的方法，利用数学模型引导大语言模型模拟人类在策略互动中的多样化决策行为（如贝叶斯更新、动机性推理等），并在法律说服博弈中验证其有效性。结果显示，大模型可通过提示近似复杂认知模型，而小模型则需结合强化学习训练（Equation-to-Behavior RL）才能有效模仿。该方法显著降低信念误差，并提升小模型在多样化决策者环境下的表现，为更真实的人类行为模拟提供支持，也拓展了对复杂认知模型的研究可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在安全评估和训练中使用的虚拟人类行为过于单一，无法覆盖人类在战略互动中的多样决策模式（如贝叶斯更新与认知偏差并存），亟需更全面的建模工具以增强仿真真实性。

Method: 提出Equation-to-Behavior Prompting方法，通过数学方程指导大模型生成符合特定认知模型的行为；对小模型则采用Equation-to-Behavior RL，即基于数学规则的强化学习训练，使其逼近目标行为模式。

Result: 大模型在提示下可有效模拟多种认知模型；小模型经强化学习训练后，信念误差降低26.5%；在多样化决策者训练环境下，平均信念变化提升2.5%–12%，优于仅基于贝叶斯模型的训练。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了将数学认知模型融入大语言模型行为生成的可行性，不仅提升了人类行为仿真的多样性与真实性，也为未来构建更复杂、更贴近真实人类心理的智能系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: People make decisions differently in strategic interactions. Some update beliefs like a Bayesian; others exhibit biases like motivated reasoning. Although creators of large language models use simulated humans for safety evaluations and training, they often fail to cover this breadth of human behavior. We argue that cognitive science and economics provide a convenient tool for doing so, making use of mathematical models of human decision-making. We propose an approach that we call Equation-to-Behavior Prompting for guiding large language models to match cognitive models, and evaluate this approach on persuasion games based on legal decision-making. We find that large models can approximate equation-based specifications -- Bayesian updating, affine distortion, motivated updating, and Grether's $α$-$β$ model -- using prompting, but small models fail to do so. However, training small models with reinforcement learning to adhere to mathematical rules, Equation-to-Behavior RL, reduces belief error by 26.5% in out-of-distribution parameterizations. We show that these simulations can help create diverse training environments; training small models to consider different kinds of decision-makers improves average belief change by 2.5%--12% over Bayesian-only training, even when persuading GPT-5-mini. Our work could improve human simulations for training and evaluation in increasingly realistic settings, and could also enable novel research into more complicated mathematical models of human decision-making.

Abstract: Parametric computer-aided design records both final geometry and the ordered construction history that determines how a part can be edited. We introduce FllumaOne, a code-native multimodal CAD dataset whose models are generated by executable Python programs in Flluma, a Qt/C++ OpenCASCADE-based CAD system. Each sample aligns its program with a structured feature tree, a training-oriented intermediate representation, STEP geometry, a surface point cloud, natural-language descriptions, metadata, and eight canonical visible-edge renderings.

Programs are executed and retained only after kernel geometry, solid validity, and export checks; release reports also record modality completeness and split-level duplicate tests. For the 9,909 predictions converted to surface point clouds, the mean normalized Chamfer Distance is 0.002124. The dataset supports conditioned CAD reconstruction, executable program synthesis, feature-tree prediction, B-Rep analysis, retrieval, design completion, and editable reverse engineering.

### [168] [EComAgentBench: Benchmarking Shopping Agents on Long-Horizon Tasks with Distributed Hidden Intent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17698)
*Zeyao Du,Tong Li,Haibo Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EComAgentBench是一个基于真实亚马逊产品和评论的662个任务的基准测试，旨在模拟购物者需求在查询、个人资料和澄清对话中逐步揭示的真实场景。该基准要求智能体在100次工具调用内挖掘隐藏意图、验证候选商品的属性与评论证据，并做出最终选择。通过带类型和来源标签的评分标准，可精准定位每个失败的原因。自动化构建确保可靠性，所有答案预先固定于代码中。对七种模型的评估显示最强模型仅达57.1%准确率，且对隐藏需求的满足度显著下降。该基准推动购物代理从单次查询向长期可靠协助演进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法捕捉购物需求在查询、用户档案或提问过程中逐步显现的真实场景，导致无法有效评估智能体在长周期任务中的表现及失败原因。

Method: 构建一个包含662个任务的自动化基准EComAgentBench，任务设计将需求分散于可见查询、工具控制的用户档案和脚本化澄清环节；使用带类型和来源标签的评分体系逐项评估每项需求的满足情况；所有答案预先编码验证，确保构建可靠性。

Result: 评估显示，即使最强模型整体准确率也仅为57.1%，且对隐藏来源需求的满足度明显低于可见需求。该基准能有效揭示模型在长周期任务中的短板，为未来研究提供可复现的基础。

Conclusion: EComAgentBench为购物代理提供了可复现的评估基础，推动其从单次搜索向长期、可靠的交互式协助演进。

Abstract: As LLM-based shopping agents enter production, existing benchmarks fail to capture how a shopper's requirements arrive: stated implicitly in the query, recorded in a profile, or revealed only when the right question is asked. Benchmarks that expose full intent upfront and grade only the final choice can neither pose this long-horizon challenge nor explain which requirement an agent missed. To address this gap, we introduce EComAgentBench, a benchmark of 662 tasks grounded in real Amazon products and reviews. Each task scatters these requirements across a visible query, a tool-gated profile, and scripted clarification; an agent must uncover hidden intent, verify candidates against attributes and review evidence, and commit to a single product within 100 tool calls. Moreover, typed, source-tagged rubrics grade every task, attributing each failure to a requirement and its source. Construction is automated yet reliable, with every answer fixed in code before any text is generated and every sample validated. Our evaluation of seven models reveals that even the strongest attains only 57.1% overall accuracy, and rubric satisfaction degrades from visible to hidden sources. Overall, we believe EComAgentBench will serve as a reproducible foundation for moving shopping agents from single-query search toward dependable assistance over long horizons.
