### [169] [LongWebBench: Evaluating Structural and Functional Webpage Generation in Long-Horizon Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17727)
*Yi Zhao,Zhen Yang,Mengpan Chen,Mingde Xu,Shanghui Gong,Xijun Liu,Jibing Gong,Jie Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出LongWebBench基准，用于评估从视觉输入生成长网页的结构和功能表现，涵盖490个真实长网页的结构保真度评估和507个目标导向的交互任务的功能评估。采用基于VLM的多维指标与DOM增强的代理式流程进行评估，并通过人工一致性分析验证自动评估的有效性。实验表明，随着网页长度增加，结构保真度下降，且视觉上看似合理的内容常无法支持多步可执行交互，强调需以可执行交互为核心评价标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型在生成网页方面取得进展，但评估主要集中在短、单屏、静态网页，缺乏对长网页在结构和功能上的全面评估。因此需要一个能衡量长网页生成质量的综合性基准。

Method: 设计LongWebBench基准，包含真实世界长网页数据集；使用多维度VLM-based指标评估结构连贯性，结合DOM增强的代理式管道进行端到端功能验证；通过人类评估分析自动评估协议的一致性。

Result: 实验结果显示，随着网页长度增加，结构保真度显著下降；即使生成结果视觉上合理，也往往无法支持多步交互任务；自动评估方法与人工判断具有较高一致性，证明其有效性。

Conclusion: 当前视觉语言模型在长网页生成中面临结构性退化与功能性缺失问题，必须超越仅依赖视觉相似性的评估方式，将可执行交互作为核心评价标准，推动更高质量的长网页生成技术发展。

Abstract: Recent vision-language models (VLMs) have shown promising progress in generating webpages from visual inputs, yet existing evaluations mainly focus on short, single-screen, and largely static webpages. We introduce LongWebBench, a benchmark for evaluating long-horizon webpage generation from both structural and functional perspectives. LongWebBench contains 490 real-world long webpages for structural fidelity evaluation and 507 goal-oriented interaction tasks over 129 webpages for functional evaluation. It employs two complementary protocols: a multi-dimensional VLM-based metric for assessing long-range structural coherence, and a DOM-augmented agent-based pipeline for end-to-end functional verification. We further examine the automatic evaluation protocols through human agreement analysis. Experiments with state-of-the-art open-source and proprietary VLMs under single-image and multi-image settings reveal that structural fidelity degrades as webpage length increases, while visually plausible generations often fail to support executable multi-step interactions. These results highlight the need to evaluate long webpage generation beyond visual similarity, with executable interaction as a core criterion. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/zheny2751-dotcom/LongWebBench.

### [170] [Shattering the Autoregressive Curse: Dynamic Epistemic Entropy Orchestrated Erasable Reinforcement Learning for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17735)
*Ziliang Wang,Kang An,Faqiang Qian,Jialu Cai,Cijun Ouyang,Yuhang Wang,Qibing Ren,Yichao Wu*

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型在长序列逻辑推理中因自回归特性导致的早期错误传播问题，提出动态认知熵可擦除强化学习（E³RL）。该方法通过内生自回归交叉熵作为认知不确定性度量，引入分段自适应动态阈值与优势分配机制，实现对局部逻辑缺陷的精准修正，并复用历史键值缓存流，赋予模型自愈能力。在DeepMath-103k数据集上训练后，E³RL显著提升探索效率与样本效率，保持线性内存开销，在AIME等数学推理基准上分别以4B和8B模型超越SOTA 5.349%和6.514%，证明其有效打破自回归诅咒，为下一代自愈型通用人工智能奠定理论与系统基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服大语言模型在长序列逻辑推理中因自回归特性引发的早期错误传播问题，避免小的认知扰动导致后续推理链崩溃。

Method: 提出E³RL，利用模型内部自回归交叉熵作为认知不确定性的内在坐标，结合分段自适应动态阈值与优势分配机制，实现局部逻辑缺陷的精准修复，并复用历史键值缓存流以支持自愈能力。

Conclusion: E³RL成功打破长序列推理中的自回归诅咒，为下一代具备自愈能力的通用人工智能提供了理论与系统层面的基础。

Abstract: Although reinforcement learning (RL) has expanded the cognitive boundaries of large language models (LLMs), it often remains vulnerable to the autoregressive curse in long-horizon logical reasoning: small epistemic perturbations introduced early in generation can propagate irreversibly along the Markov decision process flow, triggering cascading failures that drive the reasoning trajectory toward collapse. To overcome this autoregressive cascade, in which a single early mistake can compromise all subsequent reasoning steps, we propose dynamic epistemic entropy orchestrated erasable reinforcement learning ($\text{E}^3\text{RL}$). $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ eliminates reliance on external signals by grounding the model's endogenous local autoregressive cross-entropy as an intrinsic coordinate of epistemic uncertainty. By introducing segment-level adaptive dynamic thresholds and advantage allocation, $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ enables the model to precisely excise localized logical defects while reusing historical key-value (KV) cache streams, thereby endowing the reasoning process with a self-healing capability. We train $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ on the DeepMath-103k dataset. Experimental results show that $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ reshapes the exploration efficiency of long-sequence reasoning and improves sample efficiency while maintaining linear memory overhead. On mathematical reasoning benchmarks such as AIME, $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ achieves substantial performance gains, with the 4B and 8B parameter models surpassing previous state-of-the-art (SOTA) results by 5.349\% and 6.514\%, respectively. These findings suggest that $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ shatters the autoregressive curse in long-sequence reasoning and establishes a theoretical and systems-level foundation for the next generation of self-healing artificial general intelligence (AGI).

### [171] [DecoSearch: Complexity-Aware Routing and Plan-Level Repair for Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17821)
*Esteban Schafir,Xu Zheng,Hojat Allah Salehi,Zhuomin Chen,Mo Sha,Wei Cheng,Dongsheng Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DecoSearch 是一个无需训练的框架，通过动态路由查询至合适的推理层级来提升复杂SQL生成能力。它结合轻量级模式选择器、LLM判断器、RAG组件和拓扑修正器，实现高效且准确的多步推理，显著优于现有无训练基线，在BIRD和Spider数据集上分别达到70.53%和88.31%的执行准确率，同时大幅减少令牌消耗，并可作为通用封装提升各类微调模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型的自然语言转SQL方法在处理需要多步、数据感知推理的复杂查询时表现不佳，亟需一种无需训练即可增强推理能力的解决方案。

Method: DecoSearch采用分层推理机制：首先使用轻量级模式选择器筛选相关表与列；接着由LLM判断器决定是否需要分解问题；简单问题直接生成SQL，复杂问题则通过有向无环图（DAG）分解为原子子问题，并逐个求解；RAG组件提供语义相似的训练示例以辅助分解，拓扑修正器在执行失败时重构推理路径。

Result: 在BIRD数据集上实现70.53%的执行准确率，在Spider数据集上达到88.31%的执行准确率（使用DeepSeek作为骨干模型），显著超越所有训练-free基线，且消耗的令牌数量少一个数量级；同时可作为模型无关的封装，无需修改即可提升微调模型的表现。

Conclusion: DecoSearch通过智能推理路径选择与动态分解机制，有效提升了大语言模型在复杂SQL生成任务中的表现，是一种高效、通用且无需训练的先进解决方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in translating natural language to SQL, yet existing methods still falter on complex queries requiring multi-step, data-aware reasoning. We introduce DecoSearch, a training-free framework that addresses this by routing each query to the appropriate level of reasoning effort. A lightweight Schema Selector first prunes the full database schema to the relevant tables and columns. An LLM Judger then decides whether the question requires decomposition: straightforward questions follow a direct generation path and complex ones are escalated to a Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) of atomic sub-questions, each solved by a targeted SQL generation step. A RAG component grounds the decomposer with semantically similar training examples, and a Topology Refiner restructures the reasoning plan when execution failures signal a flawed decomposition rather than a fixable SQL error. DecoSearch achieves 70.53% execution accuracy on BIRD and 88.31% on Spider with a DeepSeek backbone, surpassing all training-free baselines while consuming an order of magnitude fewer tokens than competing methods. It also functions as a model-agnostic wrapper, consistently improving fine-tuned SQL generation backbones without any modification to the pipeline.

### [173] [A homotopy-type-theoretic generalization of neurosymbolic inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17851)

TL;DR: 该论文提出将神经符号系统中的信念加权求和函数从基于集合的框架改进为基于同伦类型论中类型的框架，引入信念加权同伦基数的概念，以保留对称性和证明数量的信息。通过构建新框架并证明保守性定理，表明在无对称性时可还原经典结果，并揭示了推理捷径背后的对称性。实证显示，仅用单模型在对称群上平均即可实现更优校准，优于多样性训练的集成方法，且保持准确率与可识别概念不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经符号系统基于集合，忽略了理论对称性以及证明数量等重要信息，导致无法充分捕捉推理捷径的本质。为提升系统的表达力和校准能力，需引入能保留对称性信息的新数学结构。

Method: 采用同伦类型论中的类型替代传统集合，定义信念加权同伦基数；构建完整的神经符号计算框架，证明其在平凡对称情况下的保守性；利用对称群平均推导出对称不变的后验分布。

Result: 提出的框架能够精确建模推理捷径所依赖的对称性，单一模型经对称群平均后，在MNIST推理基准上表现优于集成方法，校准性更好，同时保持原有精度和概念可识别性。

Conclusion: 通过将基础数学结构从集合替换为类型，神经符号系统得以显式处理对称性，从而实现更准确、更可解释的推理。该框架不仅理论完备，且在实践中显著提升了模型校准性，为未来神经符号系统设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: A wide range of neurosymbolic (NeSy) systems compute one functional: a belief-weighted sum of a logical quantity over a space of $σ$-structures, of which weighted model counting, fuzzy logic, and probabilistic logic are special cases. This account is built on sets, and a set deliberately forgets two things that are important for NeSy: when two $σ$-structures are the same up to a symmetry of the theory, and how many distinct proofs witness a query. Replacing the underlying sets by types, in the sense of homotopy type theory, preserves this information, and turns this functional into a belief-weighted homotopy cardinality, a notion of size that counts each object in inverse proportion to its symmetries. We develop the framework from scratch for NeSy systems, prove a conservativity theorem that recovers the classical functional when symmetries are trivial, and show that the symmetry our framework exposes is exactly the one behind reasoning shortcuts. The payoff is concrete: the shortcut-aware concept posterior that recent methods reach by ensembling or expressive density estimation is the only symmetry-invariant point of the confusion-set simplex, computable in closed form by averaging a single model over the symmetry group. On MNIST reasoning-shortcut benchmarks this single-model wrapper is better calibrated than a diversity-trained ensemble, while leaving label accuracy and identifiable concepts untouched. Code is freely available at https://github.com/bio-ontology-research-group/hott-nesy.

### [174] [FlowRAG: Synergizing Explicit Reasoning via Frequency-Aware Multi-Granularity Graph Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17856)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建四级异构图（段落、摘要、句子、实体），以摘要节点为语义枢纽；采用双粒度激活模块融合摘要-查询对齐与句子级匹配；引入频率加权流模块，根据段内词频加权实体-段落链接，剔除噪声连接，提取显式逻辑骨架用于生成。

Result: 在多个复杂推理基准测试中，FlowRAG 达到当前最优性能，显著提升了语义召回率与多跳推理的稳定性与可靠性。

Abstract: Graph-based retrieval-augmented generation (GraphRAG) is effective for knowledge-intensive and multi-hop query tasks; however, many existing methods primarily seed entity-based graphs and rely on implicit semantic relevance propagation. This often (i) under-retrieves when user queries are abstract and semantically sparse at the entity level, and (ii) suffers from brittle multi-hop reasoning, where noisy activations can derail entity-to-entity transitions and corrupt the inferred relation chain, yielding unreliable conclusions. To this end, we propose \texttt{FlowRAG}, a semantic-aware retrieval framework that improves both semantic recall and explicit reasoning. Specifically, \texttt{FlowRAG} constructs a quad-level heterogeneous graph over passages, summaries, sentences, and entities, where summary nodes serve as a coarse semantic hub. At retrieval time, a dual-granularity activation module combines summary--query alignment with sentence-level matching to activate relevant entities under paraphrase and abstraction robustly. We then introduce a frequency-aware weighted flow module that routes relevance through entity--passage links weighted by within-passage term frequency, pruning noisy connections and extracting high-confidence reasoning paths as an explicit logic skeleton for generation. Extensive experiments show that \texttt{FlowRAG} obtains state-of-the-art performance on complex reasoning benchmarks.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网页导航方法因奖励错位和误差传播导致单步脆弱性，难以有效应对复杂自然语言目标下的交互任务。

Method: 设计Dynamic Dual-Policy Optimization（DDPO）以动态切换探索与回答优先模式，缓解奖励冲突；引入Confidence-Guided Adaptive Navigation Reflection（CANR）机制，基于每步置信度触发反思并使用对比奖励促进自我校正，实现单步校准。

Result: 在标准网页导航基准上显著提升导航与答案准确率，达到新的状态--of-the-art性能。

Abstract: Web navigation requires agents to follow natural language goals, interact with web pages, and produce accurate answers. While recent advances leverage vision-language models and reinforcement learning, existing methods still suffer from single-step fragility due to reward misalignment and error propagation. To tackle the reward entanglement, we design Dynamic Dual-Policy Optimization (DDPO), which dynamically switches between a navigation-first mode for exploration and an answer-first mode for question-answering to mitigate reward conflict. To calibrate the single-step error, we propose Confidence-Guided Adaptive Navigation Reflection (CANR), a mechanism that estimates per-step confidence, triggers reflection only when necessary, and uses contrastive rewards to encourage self-correction to calibrate the single-step inaccuracy. With the above as the main components, we finally develop our StepGuard, a new framework of Guarding Web Navigation via Single-Step Calibration. Experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly improves navigation and answer accuracy, setting new state-of-the-art performance on standard web navigation benchmarks.

### [176] [Structural Preservation and the Logical Expressiveness of Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17882)
*Przemysław Andrzej Wałęga,Bernardo Cuenca Grau*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文从语义角度研究图神经网络（GNN）分类器的逻辑表达能力，探讨其在结构保持性质（如嵌入、单射同态、同态）下的不变性。研究发现，每种性质对应一个特定的广义模态逻辑片段：嵌入对应存在性广义模态逻辑，单射同态对应其存在性正片段，同态对应存在性正模态逻辑。这些结果不依赖于具体架构选择，且每个类别均存在具有相同表达力的GNN架构。技术上引入了有界高度树的新良基序结果，实现展开不变类的有限表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作多基于特定架构设计建立GNN与逻辑形式系统的对应关系，但缺乏对更广泛类别的GNN表达力的统一刻画。本文旨在从语义出发，揭示不同结构不变性条件下GNN分类器的逻辑表达能力，摆脱对具体架构的依赖，提供更具普遍性的理论框架。

Method: 采用语义视角分析GNN在嵌入、单射同态和同态下的不变性，结合模型论中的展开不变性概念，利用有界高度树上的新良基序结果，构造有限表示，并通过逻辑片段（如存在性广义模态逻辑）来刻画对应的GNN类别。

Result: 证明了三种结构不变性分别对应三种逻辑片段：存在性广义模态逻辑、其存在性正片段、存在性正模态逻辑；并展示了每个逻辑片段都可由相应结构的GNN架构实现，且该架构具有相同表达力。

Conclusion: 本研究为图神经网络的表达能力提供了不依赖具体架构的语义化逻辑刻画，揭示了结构不变性与逻辑表达力之间的深层联系，同时证明了这些表达力可通过合理的GNN架构实现，推动了GNN与逻辑系统之间理论桥梁的深化。

Abstract: Bridges between graph neural networks (GNNs) and logical formalisms have been established by fixing architectural choices, such as the types of aggregation, combination, and activation functions. These choices define restricted classes of GNNs for which tight correspondences with logical formalisms can be obtained, by showing that logical formulae can be translated into equivalent GNNs and, conversely, that GNNs can be translated into equivalent formulae.
  In this paper we take a semantic perspective by establishing the logical expressiveness of classes of GNN classifiers that are preserved under structural properties: embeddings (extensions), injective homomorphisms, and homomorphisms. We show that, for each such property, there exists a fragment of graded modal logic characterising the class of GNNs. In particular, preservation under embeddings, injective homomorphisms, and homomorphisms corresponds to existential graded modal logic, its existential-positive fragment, and existential-positive modal logic, respectively. These results characterise the expressiveness of broad classes of GNNs independently of specific architectural choices, but we also show that each of these classes admits a GNN architecture of the same expressiveness.
  Technically, our approach uses a new well-quasi-order result for trees of bounded height, yielding finite representations of unravelling-invariant classes.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将视觉输入视为同质或辅助信号，未能捕捉文本与图像在数学问题求解中的复杂且样本特定的依赖关系，导致监督信号粗略、训练反馈不准确，影响模型实现精准的多模态推理。

Method: 构建MathVis-Fine数据集，包含细粒度视觉标注与视觉依赖评分；提出两阶段渐进式视觉增强训练范式，依据每个样本的内在视觉依赖水平动态调整答案正确性奖励与视觉定位奖励的比例，以减少奖励偏差并提升监督准确性。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提框架能够根据视觉依赖程度逐步增强视觉感知，显著改善多模态数学推理中的视觉理解能力，提供更精确的训练支持。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一个有效的细粒度视觉依赖建模框架，解决了多模态数学推理中视觉监督不精准的问题，推动了对视觉信息在复杂推理任务中作用的深入理解，并为未来研究提供了高质量数据集和训练范式。

Abstract: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning has extended from purely linguistic domains to multimodal scenarios; however, existing approaches often treat visual inputs as homogeneous or auxiliary signals, failing to capture the intricate and sample-specific dependencies between text and images in mathematical problem-solving. This gives rise to two core issues: first, the supervisory signals for visual content are generalized and coarse-grained, lacking adaptation to the actual necessity of visual information in each sample; second, training feedback becomes inaccurate when visual rewards are uniformly applied without distinguishing the complementary relationships among inputs. These limitations hinder models from achieving precise multimodal reasoning. In this work, we propose a framework for modeling fine-grained visual dependencies in mathematical reasoning. We first construct the MathVis-Fine dataset, augmenting fine-grained visual annotations with visual dependency ratings. Building upon this dataset, we introduce a two-stage progressive visual enhancement training paradigm that balances answer correctness rewards and visual grounding rewards according to the intrinsic visual dependency level of each sample, thereby mitigating reward bias and improving supervision accuracy. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the MathVis-Fine framework effectively enhances visual perception progressively based on visual dependency, offering a more precise training framework for multimodal mathematical reasoning. We will release the dataset upon acceptance.

Conclusion: 当前基于规程的语言模型在处理偏离路径的用户查询时存在显著缺陷，其倾向选择看似合理但错误的建议，而非明确拒绝，凸显了对更鲁棒、可解释的拒绝机制的需求，也强调了建立更具现实挑战性的评估基准的重要性。

Abstract: Language models increasingly serve as advisory systems in maintenance operations. Evaluating a panel of ten commercial and open-weight models reveals high variability in abstention rates, with models commonly selecting a real but contextually inadequate step rather than fabricating facts. ### [180] [PreAct: Computer-Using Agents that Get Faster on Repeated Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17929)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PreAct 是一种让计算机使用代理在重复任务时更快的方法。首次成功后，它将操作编译为小型状态机程序，后续运行直接重播该程序，速度提升8.5-13倍，且无需每步调用语言模型。重播过程中会检查屏幕状态是否匹配预期，若不一致则交还控制权给代理。PreAct 通过独立评估器验证程序有效性，防止错误程序累积，显著提升任务成功率。实验表明，提示词、运行时限制或选择程序的模型类型对效果影响不大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理在重复任务时仍从头开始推理和操作，效率低下；需要一种机制来利用过往经验，加速重复任务的执行，同时保证可靠性。

Method: PreAct 在首次成功完成任务后，将操作序列编译为状态机程序（包含屏幕状态检查与动作转换），后续运行直接重播该程序。重播前进行状态匹配验证，若不一致则回退至原始代理。新程序在存入存储前需经独立评估器验证其有效性，确保能真正完成任务。

Result: 在移动、桌面和网页三个基准测试中，PreAct 相比基线方法平均提升1.75-2.6个任务的成功率，且重播速度提升8.5-13倍，无每步语言模型调用开销。不同策略如提示词、运行时约束、程序选择方式对性能影响较小。

Conclusion: PreAct 有效提升了重复任务的执行效率与可靠性，通过状态机重播与程序验证机制，在不依赖复杂模型的前提下实现显著加速与稳定表现，证明了可复用程序的长期价值。

Abstract: Computer-using agents drive real software through the screen -- clicking and typing -- but they solve every task from scratch: asked to repeat a task, an agent re-reads the screen, re-reasons every tap, and pays the full cost again. We present PreAct, which lets such an agent get faster on tasks it has done before. The first time it succeeds, PreAct compiles the run into a small state-machine program-states that check the screen, transitions that act-and on later runs replays it directly instead of invoking the agent 8.5-13x faster, with no per-step language-model calls. Replay is not blind: at each step PreAct checks that the screen matches what the program expects before acting, and hands control back to the agent the moment something is off.
  PreAct applies the same discipline when deciding what to keep: a freshly compiled program enters the store only if, re-run from a clean state, an independent evaluator confirms it solved the task-catching programs that replay to their last step yet leave the task undone. Across a mobile, a desktop, and a web benchmark, this store-time check separates repeated runs that improve from ones that degrade as faulty programs accumulate, worth 1.75-2.6 tasks per benchmark, the same direction on all three; a fallback that explores afresh when no program fits brings PreAct level with a strong record-and-replay baseline. We also report what did not matter: prompt wording, runtime guardrails, and whether a language model or a plain embedding retriever selects which program to reuse.

</details>


### [181] [How Inference Compute Shapes Frontier LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17930)
*Jessica McFadyen,Ole Jorgensen,Harry Coppock,Kevin Wei,Cozmin Ududec*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了在不同推理计算资源下前沿语言模型在多个挑战性基准测试中的表现，发现更大的上下文预算、上下文压缩和重复提交尝试等推理扩展方法能显著提升性能。评估结果表明，固定预算的评测可能低估模型的真实能力，尤其对于较新模型而言。不同基准对不同推理策略的响应差异明显，因此评测应报告模型能力随推理计算的变化，并明确说明协议选择，以更公平地比较模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI评估正转向需要更长轨迹和工具使用的复杂任务，而模型表现越来越依赖于测试时可用的计算资源。然而，多数评估仅在单一受限预算下报告性能，导致低分可能反映的是评估设置而非模型真实能力，因此亟需重新审视评估方法。

Method: 在七个涵盖软件工程、数学、医学和网络安全的挑战性基准上，评估12个前沿语言模型。采用三种可控的推理扩展干预措施：更大的令牌预算、上下文压缩和由模型自身或少量正确性反馈引导的重复提交尝试。通过系统性实验分析不同策略对性能的影响。

Result: 1. 更大的令牌预算显著提升多领域基准的表现；2. 固定预算评估会逐渐低估先进模型的能力，尤其在大预算下模型可解决更难任务并更可靠地完成；3. 不同基准对推理扩展方法的敏感度不同，重复提交普遍有效，但大预算、外部反馈和并行尝试的价值因任务而异。

Conclusion: 基准测试得分高度依赖评估协议，建议未来评估应报告模型能力随推理计算的变化，明确说明协议选择，并在相同计算范围内进行跨代模型比较，特别是在安全或政策相关场景中。

Abstract: AI evaluations are shifting toward harder tasks that benefit from longer trajectories involving tool use and iterative problem solving. As a result, performance is increasingly sensitive to the amount and allocation of compute available at test time ("inference compute"). Yet many evaluations still report performance at a single restrictive budget, meaning that low scores may reflect the evaluation setup rather than the model's underlying capability. To test this, we evaluate up to 12 frontier language models on seven challenging benchmarks spanning software engineering, mathematics, medicine, and cybersecurity. We use a controlled setup combining three simple inference-scaling interventions: larger token budgets, context compaction, and repeated submission attempts, guided either by the model itself or by minimal correctness feedback. We find three main results. First, larger token budgets substantially improve performance on benchmarks across multiple domains, including cybersecurity, FrontierMath, Humanity's Last Exam, and TerminalBench. Second, fixed-budget evaluations can increasingly understate frontier capability as models advance. Newer models reach higher performance at large budgets, where they unlock harder tasks and solve them more reliably. Third, benchmarks differ in which inference-scaling methods help most: repeated submission broadly improves performance, but the value of larger token budgets, external feedback, and parallel attempts varies by benchmark. Overall, our results show that benchmark scores are protocol-dependent. We therefore argue that evaluations should report capability as a function of inference-time compute, specify protocol choices explicitly, and compare model generations over a large shared compute range at matched budgets, especially in safety- or policy-relevant settings.

Method: 通过系统实验分析不同初始化尺度对模型预训练的影响，识别出限制小初始化优势的两个常见设置，并提出改进方法；结合机制分析和分词级别评估，揭示小初始化如何引导参数发展出压缩-扩展的轨迹，从而提升推理性能。

Abstract: Large language models provide a tractable system for asking how intelligence itself emerges, rather than only how LLMs can be engineered. Although progress is usually attributed to scale, data and architecture, we show that parameter initialization is a gene-like determinant of training and, in particular, of model capacity. Reducing the initialization scale consistently improves pretraining, with the largest gains on reasoning-demanding tasks. We identify two widely used empirical settings that restrain the advantage of small initialization, and show how relaxing them restores favorable scaling. We further uncover a critical initialization that balances the reasoning and training. Mechanistically, small initialization drives a distinct developmental trajectory: parameters first condense into low-complexity structures and later expand into richer representations, giving concrete form to the idea that compression is intelligence. Token-level analyses show that the gains concentrate on non-trivial, context-constrained predictions rather than all tokens uniformly. These results motivate a simple $γ$-initialization rule: expose initialization rage as an explicit knob and use small initialization by default, an almost cost-free intervention that improves pretraining and strengthens reasoning across model scales.

### [184] [STAR: SpatioTemporal Adaptive Reward Allocation for Text-to-Image RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17979)
*Jinjie Shen,Wei Deng,Xian Hu,Daiguo Zhou,Jian Luan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出SpatioTemporal Adaptive Reward (STAR)分配方法，通过利用文本-图像注意力机制，动态生成随去噪步骤和回放变化的空间分配图，将相同组内相对优势分配给更相关的潜在区域，几乎无额外计算开销。STAR通过空间解析的策略目标对这些区域施加强化更新，提升文本到图像生成中的语义对齐、文本渲染和偏好优化，在GenEval、OCR和PickScore上分别取得0.9759、0.9757和23.60的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习后训练方法将最终图像奖励转换为单一标量优势，并以相同强度应用于整个生成轨迹，但文本到图像生成具有时间和空间结构：不同去噪步骤负责不同生成阶段，真正决定文本对齐的内容仅出现在图像部分区域。这种粒度不匹配导致策略更新难以聚焦于实际影响奖励的生成组件。

Method: STAR利用生成模型内部的文本-图像注意力，从用户提示中真正关心的核心内容出发，构建动态变化的空间分配图，根据相关性在去噪步骤和回放中分配组内相对优势，并通过空间解析的策略目标对高相关区域施加强策略更新，实现高效且精准的奖励分配。

Result: 在Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium基础上，于GenEval、OCR文本渲染和PickScore三个任务上评估，STAR显著提升了组合语义对齐、文本渲染质量与偏好优化能力，分别达到0.9759、0.9757和23.60的得分，且无需改变外部奖励源。

Conclusion: STAR通过时空自适应奖励分配机制，有效解决了文本到图像生成中奖励信号粒度不匹配的问题，实现了更精准、高效的策略更新，显著提升生成质量，具备广泛适用性与低计算开销优势。

Abstract: Existing RL post-training methods for text-to-image generation usually convert the final-image reward into a single scalar advantage and apply it with the same strength to the entire generative trajectory. However, text-to-image generation naturally has temporal and spatial structure: different denoising steps are responsible for different generation stages, and the content that truly determines text alignment often appears only in part of the image. This granularity mismatch makes it difficult for policy updates to focus on the generative components that actually affect the reward. To address this issue, we propose \textbf{SpatioTemporal Adaptive Reward (STAR) Allocation} for RL post-training of text-to-image diffusion and flow models. STAR uses text-image attention inside the generative model and starts from the core content that the user truly cares about in the prompt. It constructs spatial allocation maps that dynamically vary across denoising steps and rollouts, and allocates the same group-relative advantage to more relevant latent regions with almost no additional computational overhead. STAR then applies stronger policy updates to these regions through a spatially resolved policy objective. We use Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium as the base model and evaluate on three tasks: GenEval, OCR text rendering, and PickScore. Experimental results show that STAR improves compositional semantic alignment, text rendering, and preference optimization without changing the external reward source, achieving $\mathbf{0.9759}$, $\mathbf{0.9757}$, and $\mathbf{23.60}$ on GenEval, OCR, and PickScore, respectively.

</details>


### [185] [LLM Consumer Behavior Theory: Foundations of a Novel Research Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18005)
*Manon Reusens,Sofie Goethals,David Martens*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出“大语言模型消费者行为理论”，旨在研究基于大语言模型的代理在市场中的消费行为，统一了以往关于大语言模型决策、人类行为模拟和偏好获取的研究，从经济学视角分析代理如何反映和执行人类偏好，并探讨其对市场总需求的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型被越来越多地用作自主代理代表用户做出消费决策，传统以人类为中心的消费者理论面临挑战，亟需建立新的理论框架来理解代理市场中的行为机制。

Method: 结合经典与行为经济学及自然语言处理的最新进展，形式化分析大语言模型代理如何体现和执行人类偏好，并探讨其在市场层面的聚合效应。

Result: 提出了一个整合性的理论框架，揭示了在代理市场中理性假设和异质性假设可能失效的领域，明确了对对齐、偏好表示和市场动态等关键问题的开放性研究方向。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解大语言模型作为消费者代理的行为提供了理论基础，指明未来研究应聚焦于偏好建模、代理与人类意图的一致性以及代理市场演化机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents that make consumption decisions on behalf of users. This shift raises fundamental questions for consumer theory, which has traditionally modeled humans as the primary decision-makers. In this paper, we introduce LLM Consumer Behavior Theory, a new field of study concerned with analyzing consumer behavior in agentic markets. Drawing on classical and behavioral economics alongside recent advances in Natural Language Processing, we formalize how human preferences are reflected and acted upon by LLM-based agents, and how agent-level decisions aggregate into market demand. We unify previously fragmented literature on LLM decision-making, human behavior simulation, and preference elicitation under a common economic lens, highlighting where assumptions, such as rationality and heterogeneity, may fail in agentic markets. Rather than providing empirical validation, this paper outlines the scope of LLM consumer behavior and identifies open research questions related to alignment, preference representation, and market dynamics.

### [186] [LegalHalluLens: Typed Hallucination Auditing and Calibrated Multi-Agent Debate for Trustworthy Legal AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18021)
*Lalit Yadav,Akshaj Gurugubelli*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LegalHalluLens 是一个审计框架，用于检测法律AI系统中的幻觉问题。它包含四种法律相关声明类型的幻觉画像（数值、时间、义务/权利、事实），引入风险方向指数（RDI）以量化错误的方向性偏差，并采用经过校准的类型化辩论管道来提升检测精度。在510份合同和249,252个条款级实例上测试显示，模型在义务/数值与时间类声明间的幻觉差距达38-40个百分点，而传统平均率掩盖了这一差异。两个幻觉率均为52%的系统可能具有相反的RDI值。该框架使辩论管道减少45%的虚假生成，且性能优于商业API，仅用40亿活跃参数。诊断工具可作为多智能体辩论的校准输入，针对性策略优于通用设置。整体支持法律AI部署中的方向感知采购、问责与代理设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有法律AI系统的幻觉率平均为52%，但此平均值掩盖了错误集中领域及方向性偏差，导致合规人员无法获得可操作信号以确保可信部署。亟需一种能揭示幻觉模式、方向与严重程度的精细评估机制。

Method: 提出LegalHalluLens框架，包括：(1) 针对四类法律声明的幻觉类型化画像；(2) 风险方向指数（RDI）以统一衡量误报与漏报偏差；(3) 经校准的类型化辩论管道，结合大小模型协同推理，实现对不同类别幻觉的精准识别与抑制。

Result: 实验覆盖510份合同、249,252个条款实例，发现模型在义务/数值与时间类声明间存在约38-40个百分点的幻觉差距，而传统指标无法体现；两个幻觉率同为52%的系统可能具有相反的RDI值；辩论管道使虚构内容检测减少45%，性能媲美大型商业API，但仅使用40亿参数。诊断工具有效指导多智能体辩论的优化配置，显著提升效果。

Conclusion: LegalHalluLens通过类型化幻觉画像与方向敏感的RDI，揭示了传统聚合指标所隐藏的关键失败模式，为法律AI的可信部署提供可操作的审计能力，支持更精准的采购、问责与系统设计。

Abstract: AI systems deployed in legal workflows hallucinate at rates that aggregate metrics report at ~52%, but this average conceals where errors concentrate and in which direction they run, leaving compliance officers without an actionable signal for trustworthy deployment. We present LegalHalluLens, an auditing framework with three components: typed hallucination profiles across four legally-motivated claim categories (numeric, temporal, obligation/entitlement, factual) over CUAD (Hendrycks et al., 2021); a Risk Direction Index (RDI) that reduces omission-versus-invention bias to a single deployment-comparable scalar; and a typed debate pipeline calibrated to both magnitudes and directions. Across 510 contracts and 249,252 clause-level instances we measure a within-model gap of approximately 38-40 pp between obligation/numeric and temporal claims that aggregate reporting hides, and show that two systems with matched 52% rates can carry opposite RDIs. The debate pipeline reduces fabricated detections by 45% with per-category gains tracking the diagnosis, matching commercial APIs with a substantially smaller backbone (4B active parameters). Typed profiles and RDI surface failure modes that aggregate metrics hide; we further show these diagnostics serve as calibration inputs for multi-agent debate pipelines, where Skeptic challenges and asymmetric gates targeted at measured failure modes outperform generically-tuned debate. The framework supports direction-aware procurement, accountability, and agent design for legal AI deployed in the wild.

### [187] [ProvenanceGuard: Source-Aware Factuality Verification for MCP-Based LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18037)
*Ander Alvarez,Santhiya Rajan,Samuel Mugel,Román Orús*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ProvenanceGuard is a source-aware verifier for LLM agents using the Model Context Protocol (MCP), designed to detect cross-source conflation—where claims are supported by evidence but incorrectly attributed. It analyzes MCP traces, decomposes answers into atomic claims, routes each to its correct source, verifies support via NLI and token alignment, checks attribution accuracy, and provides per-claim verdicts and answer-level decisions. Evaluated on 281 medical-domain traces, it achieves high block F1 (0.802) and source accuracy (0.858) on held-out data, outperforming source-blind methods. On a harder multi-source benchmark, it maintains strong block F1 (0.846) despite lower source-plus-relation accuracy (0.229), indicating the challenge of precise source ownership. Repair-and-reverify resolves all blocked cases, often through conservative fallbacks. In clinical probes, it detects all attribution swaps with no false negatives.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard factuality metrics fail to detect cross-source conflation—when a claim is factually supported but wrongly attributed to a different source. This is a critical failure mode in MCP-based LLM agents that integrate heterogeneous evidence sources like search, APIs, databases, and clinical records. Accurate source attribution is essential for trust and correctness in high-stakes domains like medicine.

Method: ProvenanceGuard processes MCP traces with stable tool and source IDs and raw outputs. It breaks down answers into atomic claims, uses NLI and token-alignment proxies to check evidence support per source, compares stated attribution with the actual source of support, and generates per-claim verdicts and an overall allow/block decision. Blocked answers undergo retrieval-augmented revision and re-verification.

Result: On a 40-trace held-out test set, ProvenanceGuard achieves block F1 of 0.802 and source accuracy of 0.858 over 260 source-eligible claims. It outperforms source-blind baselines. On a more challenging multi-source benchmark, block F1 reaches 0.846, though source-plus-relation accuracy drops to 0.229, highlighting difficulty in distinguishing semantically similar sources. Repair-and-reverify successfully fixes all blocked answers. In 50 controlled clinical conflation probes, it detects all attribution swaps with no retained wrong attribution.

Conclusion: Source attribution is an independent and critical dimension of factuality verification in MCP-based LLM agents. ProvenanceGuard effectively identifies and corrects cross-source conflation, improving reliability in complex, evidence-integrating systems, especially in high-stakes medical applications.

Abstract: Tool-using LLM agents increasingly use the Model Context Protocol (MCP) to answer from heterogeneous evidence sources, including search, APIs, databases, clinical records, and formulary tools. Standard factuality metrics usually test whether an answer is supported by pooled evidence, missing a provenance-sensitive failure mode: a claim may be supported somewhere while being attributed to the wrong source. We call this cross-source conflation.
  We introduce ProvenanceGuard, a source-aware verifier for MCP-grounded answers. It consumes captured MCP traces with stable tool IDs, source IDs, and raw outputs; decomposes answers into atomic claims; routes claims to source-specific evidence; checks support with NLI and a token-alignment proxy; compares stated attribution with the routed source; and returns per-claim verdicts plus an answer-level allow/block decision. Blocked answers can be repaired with retrieval-augmented answer revision and re-verified.
  We evaluate on 281 medical-domain MCP-agent traces. A 266-trace adjudicated subset yields 2,325 LLM-assisted claim labels split by trace; 361 held-out labels are human-verified. On the 40-trace held-out split, ProvenanceGuard achieves block F1 0.802 and source accuracy 0.858 over 260 source-eligible claims, outperforming source-blind baselines that do not emit claim-to-source IDs. On a harder multi-source benchmark it reaches block F1 0.846, while source-plus-relation accuracy drops to 0.229, showing that exact source ownership remains difficult with semantically close sources. Repair-and-reverify resolves all blocked answers in the full trace set, often via conservative fallback. In 50 controlled clinical conflation probes, ProvenanceGuard detects all injected attribution swaps with no retained wrong attribution. These results show that source attribution is an independent axis for factuality verification in MCP-based agents.

</details>


### [188] [PseudoBench: Measuring How Agentic Auto-Research Fuels Pseudoscience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18060)
*Xinyang Liao,Lingyu Li,Huacan Liu,Tianle Gu,Yang Yao,Tong Zhu,Yan Teng,Yingchun Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PseudoBench是一个对抗性基准，用于评估基于大语言模型的智能体在自主科研中识别和抵制伪科学叙事的能力。该基准包含200个跨五个领域的伪科学主张-证据对，通过从实验到写作的全流程研究测试智能体。测试七种最先进的智能体发现，当前系统几乎零拒绝率地生成与伪科学前提一致的有说服力报告，最高抵抗率仅为27.4%。更强的智能体甚至会用更复杂的科学语言包装伪科学，使其更具可信度。这揭示了其助长伪科学的严重风险，呼吁在广泛部署前加强科学对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基于大语言模型的智能体进入自主科学研究领域，其抵抗伪科学的能力变得至关重要。若缺乏此能力，这些系统可能快速生成看似合理但误导性的研究，污染学术文献并削弱公众对科学的信任。因此，亟需一个评估工具来检验智能体在面对伪科学时的辨别与抵制能力。

Method: 提出PseudoBench，一个包含200个精心筛选的伪科学主张-证据对的对抗性基准，覆盖五个不同领域；通过端到端研究流程（包括实验设计、数据收集、分析与论文撰写）评估智能体的表现。

Result: 测试结果显示，当前七种主流智能体在面对伪科学前提时几乎不拒绝，生成的报告高度契合伪科学内容，最高抵抗率仅为27.4%。更强的智能体虽表现出更高水平的表达能力，却可能以更专业的科学语言包装伪科学，反而提升其欺骗性。

Conclusion: 现有智能体在抵御伪科学方面存在严重缺陷，存在被滥用以传播伪科学的风险。必须在大规模部署前强化其科学对齐机制，确保其行为符合科学伦理与实证标准。

Abstract: As Large Language Model based agents enter autonomous scientific research, their ability to resist pseudoscience becomes increasingly important. Otherwise, such systems may rapidly generate plausible yet misleading studies that contaminate academic literature and erode trust in science. We present PseudoBench, an adversarial benchmark for evaluating whether agentic auto-research systems can identify and resist pseudoscientific narratives. PseudoBench contains 200 curated pseudoscientific claim-evidence pairs across five domains and evaluates agents through an end-to-end research pipeline from experiments to writing. Testing seven state-of-the-art agents, we find that current systems readily produce persuasive reports that align with pseudoscientific premises with near-zero refusal rates and the highest resistance of only 27.4%. Stronger agents risk packaging pseudoscience in more sophisticated scientific language, increasing its apparent credibility. These findings reveal an alarming capacity to fuel pseudoscience, calling for scientific alignment before widespread deployment.

### [189] [Agentic AI-based Framework for Mitigating Premature Diagnostic Handoff and Silent Hallucination in Healthcare Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18068)
*Divyansh Srivastava,Shreya Ghosh,Anshul Verma,Rajkumar Buyya*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多智能体框架，通过确定性编排约束替代传统的LLM作为裁判的路由机制，以解决开放对话代理在医疗推理中的两大缺陷：过早诊断移交和无声的临床幻觉。该框架引入两种安全机制：1）神经符号状态跟踪门，强制执行OLDCARTS临床协议（症状的起始、部位、持续时间、性质、加重/缓解因素、放射、时间和严重程度），阻止诊断转移直至所有维度被收集；2）认知不确定性量化（UQ）门，通过计算K=5个独立诊断样本的语义熵（H）来识别并拦截分歧输出。在150个测试案例上使用Llama-3.1-70b-instruct驱动的模拟患者代理进行评估，完整架构实现49.3%的诊断精度，相比无约束基线提升11.3个百分点。同时，观察到OLDCARTS完整性（σ）与语义熵（H）之间存在显著负相关（r = -0.181, p < 0.05），表明结构化信息收集有助于降低诊断不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型的代理系统在医疗推理中存在过早诊断转移和难以察觉的临床幻觉问题，可能对患者安全构成威胁。现有方法依赖LLM作为裁判进行路由决策，缺乏可解释性和稳定性。因此需要更可靠、可验证的机制来保障医疗推理过程的完整性和准确性。

Method: 提出一个多智能体框架，采用确定性编排策略替代传统LLM裁判路由。设计两个核心安全模块：(1) 神经符号状态跟踪门，根据OLDCARTS协议动态检查是否收集了全部临床特征，未完成前禁止进入诊断阶段；(2) 基于语义熵的不确定性量化门，通过对5个独立采样的诊断结果计算熵值，检测输出分歧并提前拦截异常输出。

Result: 在150个测试案例上的实验表明，所提系统达到49.3%的诊断精度，比无约束基线提升11.3个百分点。统计分析显示，OLDCARTS完整性（σ）与语义熵（H）呈显著负相关（r = -0.181, p < 0.05），说明结构化信息采集能有效降低诊断不确定性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的多智能体框架通过确定性编排与双重安全机制，显著提升了医疗推理系统的可靠性与安全性。其核心思想——以结构化协议保障信息完整性，以不确定性量化防止幻觉输出——为构建可信的医学人工智能系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) and multi-agent systems have driven the rise of Agentic AI, showing promise for medical reasoning. However, open-ended conversational agents remain prone to two critical failure modes: premature diagnostic handoff and silent clinical hallucinations that may go undetected before reaching the patient. In this work, we propose a multi-agent framework that addresses both issues by replacing ``LLM-as-a-judge'' routing with deterministic orchestration constraints. The framework incorporates two safety mechanisms. First, a neuro-symbolic state-tracking gate enforces completeness of the OLDCARTS clinical protocol (Onset, Location, Duration, Character, Aggravating/Alleviating factors, Radiation, Timing, and Severity) by blocking diagnostic transitions until all required dimensions are collected. Second, an epistemic uncertainty quantification (UQ) gate computes semantic entropy (H) across K=5 independent diagnostic samples to identify and intercept divergent outputs before delivery.
  We evaluate the system using simulated patient agents powered by the llama-3.1-70b-instruct model on 150 test cases. The full architecture achieves 49.3% diagnostic precision, representing an absolute improvement of 11.3 percentage points over an unconstrained baseline. Additionally, we observe a statistically significant negative correlation (r = -0.181, p < 0.05) between OLDCARTS completeness (σ) and semantic entropy (H), suggesting that structured information gathering is associated with reduced diagnostic uncertainty.

### [190] [A Unified Framework for Context-Aware and Relation-Aware Graph Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18075)
*Haoyang Zhong,Yifei Sun,Antong Zhang,Chunping Wang,Lei Chen,Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HyGRAG提出了一种分层图RAG框架，通过构建混合图结构（包含块和实体节点），迭代聚类并生成基于LLM的摘要，实现上下文与关系信息的真正融合。其上下文与关系感知的检索机制可跨抽象层级搜索并扩展至社区成员，同时支持仅需局部重摘要的动态知识更新。实验表明，该方法在多跳推理任务上平均准确率提升9.7%，兼具高效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计分层索引结构于混合图（含块与实体节点），迭代聚类并生成LLM驱动的摘要；提出上下文与关系感知的检索机制，支持跨层级搜索与社区扩展；采用基于附加的算法实现动态知识更新，仅需局部重摘要。

Conclusion: HyGRAG通过分层图结构与智能摘要机制，实现了外部知识的深度融合与高效检索，为增强大语言模型的复杂推理能力提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has emerged as a paradigm for enhancing large language models (LLMs) with external knowledge, yet existing graph-based methods face a fundamental limitation: entity-centric and chunk-centric approaches operate on representations anchored to original text without true knowledge fusion. While entity-centric methods connect logically related content and chunk-centric methods preserve context, both retrieve information separately through similarity search, missing emergent understanding from their synthesis. In this paper, we propose HyGRAG, a hierarchical graph RAG framework that transcends source documents by addressing three core challenges: constructing summaries that genuinely integrate contextual and relational information, leveraging these synthesized representations to access emergent knowledge during retrieval, and efficiently updating hierarchical structures for dynamic corpora. Specifically, we design hierarchical index structures over hybrid graphs with both chunk and entity nodes, then iteratively cluster them and generate LLM-based summaries. Then, we design context and relation-aware retrieval that searches across all abstraction levels while expanding through community membership. Moreover, we enable dynamic knowledge update through attachment-based algorithms with only local re-summarization. Experimental results show that HyGRAG improves the average accuracy of multi-hop reasoning tasks by 9.7%, while maintaining reasonable efficiency.

Motivation: 传统在线自蒸馏（OPSD）在GUI接地任务中因学生生成的前缀偏离目标坐标，导致教师提供的坐标-标记信号质量下降，进而影响模型性能。因此需要一种机制来提升教师信号的质量与可靠性。

Method: 提出质量感知自蒸馏方法：使用软正确性感知门控判断当前教师坐标标记是否仍可被学生前缀完成至真实框；若不能，则降低该信号权重；同时引入教师置信度作为轻量级因子对信号强度进行校准。

Result: 在六个GUI接地基准测试中，所提方法均显著优于基线模型，且两种机制联合使用效果最佳，证明其互补性。

Conclusion: 质量感知自蒸馏通过双重机制有效提升了教师信号质量，显著增强了VLM在高精度坐标预测任务中的表现，为GUI接地提供了更可靠的训练范式。

Abstract: Graphical user interface (GUI) grounding requires vision-language models (VLMs) to identify small target elements in high-resolution screenshots and predict precise screen coordinates. On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) is a promising post-training approach for this coordinate-sensitive task, since it provides dense token-level teacher signals beyond hard coordinate labels. However, naive OPSD is not well suited to GUI grounding: OPSD evaluates the teacher on student-generated prefixes, the quality of coordinate-token teacher signals can degrade when the prefix has already deviated from the target coordinate, leading to unreliable teacher signal. To mitigate this, We propose quality-aware self-distillation for VLM-based GUI grounding, which improves coordinate-token teacher-signal quality through soft correctness-aware gating and teacher-probability scaling. The soft correctness-aware gate checks whether the teacher's current coordinate-token prediction can still be completed into the ground-truth box under the student-generated prefix. If not, the corresponding teacher signal is down-weighted. Teacher-probability scaling then uses the teacher's confidence as a lightweight factor to further calibrate the strength of the gated supervision. A key empirical finding is that neither component alone improves overall performance, whereas combining them consistently improves performance. This suggests that the two mechanisms play complementary roles: correctness-aware gating suppresses unreliable coordinate-token supervision, while teacher-probability scaling calibrates the strength of the remaining signals. Experiments across six GUI grounding benchmarks show that our method consistently improves the base model and outperforms strong baselines.

Conclusion: 当前AI系统在处理科研级数学问题时仍存在显著局限，难以独立完成从问题理解到严格证明的全过程，需依赖人类干预与指导。未来的发展需加强在形式化推理、上下文理解与创造性推导方面的能力。

Abstract: To assess the ability of current AI systems to correctly solve research-level mathematics problems, we tested several AI systems on a set of ten problems in a broad range of mathematical fields; these problems arose naturally in the research process of the contributors. This document includes the problems, our methodology, and the results of our testing. We provide links to supplementary documents including the human solutions, the AI-generated solutions, and the referee reports and logs for the AI-generated solutions.
  The ten problems were contributed by the following mathematicians: (1) Dariusz Kalociński and Theodore A. Slaman, (2) Richard Schwartz, (3) Aleksa Milojevic and Benny Sudakov, (4) Larry Guth, (5) Oleg Butkovsky, Jonathan Mattingly, and Lorenzo Zambotti, (6) Joshua Evan Greene and Duncan McCoy, (7) Sucharit Sarkar, (8) Sam Payne and Jidong (Jayden) Wang, (9) Sylvie Corteel and John Lentfer, (10) Srivatsav Kunnawalkam Elayavalli.

### [194] [Knowledge Reutilization in Meta-Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18132)
*Yuan Meng,Bo Wang,Juan de los Rios Ruiz,Xiangtong Yao,Zhenshan Bing,Fuchun Sun,Alois Knoll*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种元知识重用框架，通过在简化动力学的代理上学习任务级知识，并将其迁移到异构代理中。该框架利用贝叶斯非参数先验组织潜在任务模式，并通过高层策略生成任务级指导信号。为实现跨代理的知识复用，设计了语义-幅度接口和轻量级时间适配器，将冻结的元知识转化为与具体执行体匹配的时序子目标。实验表明，相比最新基线方法，该框架在多类运动代理上将最终步跟踪误差降低94.75%至99.79%，且仅需约23.8%的交互数据即可达到相当的部署性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端元强化学习方法常将任务推断与特定实体控制耦合，导致任务语义不清晰、样本效率低，并限制跨代理知识复用。因此需要解耦任务知识与具体执行体，以提升泛化能力与效率。

Method: 提出基于贝叶斯非参数先验的任务模式组织机制，结合高层策略生成任务级幅度指导；设计语义-幅度接口与轻量级时间适配器，实现冻结元知识向不同执行体低层控制器的时序对齐子目标转换。

Result: 在多个运动代理上的实验显示，该框架显著降低最终步跟踪误差（94.75%–99.79%），且仅需约23.8%的交互数据即达到与基线相当的部署性能，验证了其高效性与可迁移性。

Conclusion: 所提框架有效解耦任务知识与具体执行体，实现了跨代理的元知识高效重用，在保证高性能的同时大幅减少数据需求，为异构智能体快速适应新任务提供了新范式。

Abstract: Meta-reinforcement learning enables fast adaptation by extracting shared structure from related tasks, but existing end-to-end methods often couple task inference with embodiment-specific control. This coupling can obscure non-parametric task semantics, reduce sample efficiency, and limit cross-agent reuse. We propose a meta-knowledge reutilization framework that learns task-level knowledge on a dynamics-simplified agent and transfers it to heterogeneous agents. The framework uses a Bayesian non-parametric prior to organize latent task modes and a high-level policy to generate task-level magnitude guidance. To bridge reusable task knowledge with different embodiments, we introduce a semantic-magnitude interface and a lightweight temporal adaptor, which convert frozen meta-knowledge into temporally aligned subgoals for embodiment-specific low-level controllers. Experiments on multiple locomotion agents show that our framework reduces final-step tracking error by 94.75% -- 99.79% compared with recent state-of-the-art baselines and achieves comparable deployment performance with about 23.8% of their interaction data.

### [195] [Your AI Travel Agent Would Book You a Bullfight: An Agentic Benchmark for Implicit Animal Welfare in Frontier AI Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18142)
*Jasmine Brazilek,Oliver Tulio,Joel Christoph,Miles Tidmarsh,Carol Kline,Arturs Kanepajs*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出TAC（Travel Agent Compassion）基准，首个衡量AI代理在代表用户行动时是否避免涉及动物剥削选项的评估体系。通过12个精心设计的旅行预订场景（共48个样本），测试7个前沿模型在真实代理任务中的动物福利决策能力。结果显示所有模型表现均低于随机水平（64%），最佳模型Claude Opus 4.7仅达53%。引入一句福利意识提示语后，Claude和GPT-5.5性能提升47至63个百分点，而DeepSeek和Gemini提升不足12个百分点。辅助审计显示，顶级模型在无提示条件下几乎未表现出对评估任务的觉察，表明其低分非源于认知评估失败。研究揭示文本响应基准的局限性，强调需建立更符合实际应用的代理评估框架，并讨论其对文化差异及欧盟通用人工智能行为准则的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI评估多基于问答形式，无法反映模型在真实代理任务中处理动物福利等伦理问题的能力。随着AI从‘顾问’转向‘行动者’，亟需新的基准来检验其在工具使用情境下的道德决策表现。本文旨在填补这一空白，推动更负责任的AI发展。

Method: 构建TAC基准，包含12个手写旅行预订场景，覆盖六类动物剥削形式，扩展至48个样本以控制价格、评分与位置等混杂因素。评估7个来自四大机构的前沿大模型在真实代理任务中的行为表现，结合系统提示干预实验与辅助审计（Inspect Scout），利用Gemini 2.5 Flash Lite作为裁判分析288份基础条件下的对话记录。

Result: 所有模型得分均低于随机水平（64%），最佳模型为Claude Opus 4.7，仅53%。加入一句福利意识提示后，Claude与GPT-5.5性能显著提升（+47至+63个百分点），而其他模型提升有限。审计发现顶级模型在无提示条件下几乎未识别评估任务，说明其低分并非因理解评估目标。

Conclusion: 当前主流模型在代理任务中缺乏基本动物福利意识，依赖外部提示才能表现改善。文本响应基准不足以衡量真实世界中的伦理决策能力。必须发展面向代理行为的新评估范式，尤其应纳入如欧盟通用人工智能行为准则所倡导的系统性风险治理框架。

Abstract: AI agents are moving from advisors to actors, booking travel, planning menus, and running procurement on behalf of users. Existing benchmarks for AI and animal welfare evaluate model text responses to question-answer prompts, leaving open whether the welfare reasoning surfaced in those responses transfers to agentic deployment where the model must take actions with tools. We introduce TAC (Travel Agent Compassion), the first agentic benchmark measuring whether AI agents avoid options involving animal exploitation when acting on behalf of users. TAC presents an AI agent with twelve hand-authored travel booking scenarios across six categories of animal exploitation, augmented to forty-eight samples to control for price, rating, and position confounds. We evaluate seven frontier models from four labs. Every model scores below the chance level of sixty-four percent, with the best performer (Claude Opus 4.7) at fifty-three percent. A single welfare-aware sentence in the system prompt yields gains of forty-seven to sixty-three percentage points in Claude and GPT-5.5, twenty-six points in GPT-5.2, and under twelve points in DeepSeek and Gemini. An auxiliary Inspect Scout audit of 288 base-condition transcripts from the top two performers, using Gemini 2.5 Flash Lite as judge, flags zero transcripts for evaluation awareness, suggesting the below-chance rates do not stem from the models recognising the evaluation. We discuss implications for category-level variation across cultural domains, the limits of text-response welfare benchmarks, and the EU General-Purpose AI Code of Practice systemic risk framework.

### [196] [Memory as a Wasting Asset: Pricing Flash Endurance for Embodied Agents, and the Limits of Doing So](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18144)
*Josef Liyanjun Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文将机器人内存的擦写寿命视为一种不可再生的资本，提出用单一的耐久性影子价格η来定价，从而在RAM/本地NVM/云存储层级间实现成本最小化的内存放置。该方法在任意价值-写入关联符号下均最优，仅当该关联为正时，最优策略变为非单调，导致高价值记忆被移出闪存。通过真实机器人日志数据测量该关联系数χ，发现其符号取决于部署场景：长期重复操作中为正（≈+1.0×10⁻³），短期任务中为零，非重复遥控中为负。耐久性预算在高端TLC内存中不具约束力，但在低端QLC/eMMC（约1000次P/E）上具有关键影响。在有约束的情况下，学习到的磨损感知控制器仅与任务价值相关，因实际价值在各层级间不变，决定设备寿命和成本的是租金而非性能。是否磨损感知放置能提升任务价值仍待验证，因χ基于代理值测量，且非单调最优虽理论成立但尚未在数据中观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人内存系统未考虑擦写寿命的消耗，而闪存寿命是有限且不可再生的资源，因此需要一种机制来合理分配内存使用，以延长设备寿命并降低成本。现有方法缺乏对内存价值与写入行为之间关系的量化分析，无法指导高效、经济的内存管理策略。

Method: 将嵌入式内存视为一种折旧资本，引入耐久性影子价格η，构建一个考虑磨损的每字节索引，作为跨RAM/本地NVM/云层级的成本优化决策依据。通过实测机器人日志数据估计价值-写入关联系数χ，并据此判断最优内存放置策略。

Result: 在高端内存（如TLC）上，耐久性预算无约束；而在低端内存（如QLC/eMMC）上，其约束显著。当χ>0时，最优策略呈现非单调性，高价值记忆可能被移出闪存。实测显示χ在长期操作中为正，在短周期或非重复操作中接近零或为负。磨损感知控制器仅依赖任务价值进行路由，因各层级间任务价值不变，设备寿命和成本由租金决定。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于耐久性影子价格的磨损感知内存管理框架，可有效优化低成本边缘机器人中的内存使用。虽然理论上存在非单调最优策略，但其在真实数据中的表现尚待验证，未来需进一步研究磨损感知放置对任务价值的实际影响。

Abstract: A robot's flash endurance is a non-renewable stock: every persisted write spends one of a few thousand program/erase cycles and never refills, yet no fielded robot memory system prices which memories are worth an erase cycle. We treat embodied memory as depreciating capital and price that stock with a single endurance shadow price $η$, which makes cost-minimizing placement across a RAM / on-board NVM / cloud hierarchy a threshold in a wear-augmented per-byte index. The index is cost-optimal whatever the sign of the value-write association $χ$; only when $χ> 0$ does the optimum turn non-monotone, sending a robot's most valuable memories off its flash.
  The pivot is thus empirical, and we measure $χ$ on real robot logs at a pre-specified gate: its sign is a property of the deployment regime -- positive on recurrent long-horizon manipulation ($\hatχ \approx +1.0 \times 10^{-3}$, replicated at full power), null on a shorter-horizon suite, and negative on non-recurrent teleoperation. Two boundaries scope the result. The endurance budget is dormant on premium 3,000-P/E TLC at datasheet prices and binding on the commodity QLC/eMMC ($\sim$1,000 P/E) that cheaper edge robots run. And where it binds, a learned wear-aware controller only ties price-based routing on task value, because realized value is tier-invariant across RAM, NVM, and cloud: the rent governs device lifetime and cost, not task performance. Whether wear-aware placement improves task value remains open -- $χ$ is measured against a value proxy, and the non-monotone optimum, while proven, is not yet observed in data.

To address these challenges, we propose WEQA, a query-adaptive agent framework that unifies LLM reasoning with specialized wearable analytical and modeling tools. We also curate a benchmark spanning four open wearable datasets comprising analytic and predictive tasks in three different health domains. Recent works have applied large language models (LLMs) to generate or act as hybrid models. However, despite their promising generalization capacity, these LLM-based methods lack the structural priors needed for stable cardiac simulations. Hence, we propose LEADS, a framework that formulates cardiac EP domain knowledge as a structured action space and utilizes an LLM agent to discover hybrid models. The agent follows an iterative reasoning-and-action loop to select, combine, and refine hybrid models, whilst gradient descent handles parameter fitting. The proposed LEADS designs every candidate model towards physically grounded, interpretable, and numerically stable, while allowing open-ended architectural discovery. ### [199] [DRFLOW: A Deep Research Benchmark for Personalized Workflow Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18191)
*Md Tawkat Islam Khondaker,Raymond Li,Muhammad Abdul-Mageed,Laks V. S. Lakshmanan,Issam H. Laradji*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度研究系统多聚焦于生成报告和摘要，但企业级任务更需要智能体识别具体的操作流程（即一系列动作步骤）。例如，面对‘在固定预算下如何申请新增人员’的问题，智能体应能推导出具体操作步骤而非仅提供政策总结。因此，亟需一个能够评估智能体生成个性化工作流程能力的新基准。

Method: 提出DRFLOW基准，包含100个跨领域任务，每项任务要求智能体从分散来源中提取相关证据，并据此预测正确的动作序列。构建了1246个参考工作流程步骤，覆盖3900多个来源。设计七种诊断性评估指标以全面衡量工作流程的质量。开发了DRFLOW-Agent（DRFA）作为参考智能体，用于预测个性化工作流程。

Result: DRFA在多项指标上优于强基线模型，平均F1分数提升达10.02%。然而，在事实依据、步骤完整性、结构顺序、条件处理及个人化方面仍存在显著差距，表明当前技术尚未充分解决复杂工作流程的精准生成问题。

Conclusion: 预测完整且正确的个性化工作流程是深度研究中的前沿难题。尽管DRFA展现出一定进步，但整体性能仍远未达到理想水平，提示未来研究需在证据整合、逻辑推理与个性化建模方面深入探索。

Abstract: Deep research (DR) systems are increasingly used for complex information-seeking tasks, but existing works mainly focus on generating reports and summaries. In contrast, many enterprise tasks instead require an agent to identify concrete workflows which is a sequence of action-steps. For example, rather than summarizing budgeting policies, an agent should be able to determine the steps needed to answer a question such as: "How do I request new headcount given a fixed budget?". Therefore, we introduce DRFLOW, a benchmark for evaluating personalized workflows predicted by agents from heterogeneous sources. Each task requires the agent to identify relevant evidence from scattered sources, then use that evidence to predict the correct action-step sequence for the user's task. DRFLOW contains 100 tasks across five domains, with 1,246 reference workflow steps grounded in more than 3,900 sources. We define seven diagnostic metrics covering factual grounding, step recovery, structural ordering, condition resolution, and personalization. We further present DRFLOW-Agent (DRFA), a workflow-oriented reference agent to predict personalized workflow. We show that although DRFA improves over strong baseline agents (upto 10.02% average F1 score), there is substantial room for improvement remains across these workflow metrics, indicating that predicting complete and correct personalized workflows remains a challenging frontier for deep research.

</details>


### [200] [The Stanford EDGAR Filings Dataset: Reconstructing U.S. Corporate and Financial Disclosures into Layout-Faithful and Token-Efficient Pretraining Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18192)
*Nick Bettencourt,Xiaowei Ding,Kay Giesecke*

Result: SEFD-v1版本包含1520亿个标记，整体语料库规模达5500亿标记，与Common Crawl语料重合度低于0.1%，具备高度多样性与独特性。实验表明，基于SEFD训练的模型在金融推理、预测与文档理解任务上表现优异，且两个新基准有效区分了模型在真实金融场景下的能力水平。

Conclusion: SEFD成功构建了一个开放、高质量、面向金融领域的长文本语料库，填补了当前金融语言建模中真实、结构化、大规模数据的空白，为大语言模型在金融领域的应用提供了可靠的数据基础与评估标准。

Abstract: As high-quality public web corpora become increasingly exhausted, clean long-context documents have become a scarce and expensive source of training data for large language models (LLMs). Existing long-context corpora are often proprietary and costly to acquire, synthetically generated, or concentrated in narrow domains such as programming. We introduce the Stanford EDGAR Filings Dataset (SEFD), an open reconstruction of SEC filings into layout-faithful MultiMarkdown for financial language modeling and evaluation. SEFD makes audited financial statements, risk disclosures, ownership reports, accounting notes, and market-moving event filings usable as long-context pretraining data and as a basis for financial reasoning, forecasting, compliance, and document understanding. The resulting corpus is token-efficient, model-ready, and has less than 0.1% overlap with Common Crawl-derived corpora. We release SEFD-v1, a 152B-token initial public snapshot, and provide corpus-level analyses of a larger 18.5M-filing archive estimated at 550B tokens. We further introduce two SEFD-derived benchmarks: EDGAR-Forecast, which evaluates filing-grounded numerical forecasting after model knowledge cutoffs, and EDGAR-OCR, which evaluates transcription of complex financial tables.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用预归一化层与残差缩放缓解信号传播问题，设计基于Transformer的固定点推理模型（FPRM），利用固定点收敛作为端到端的停止机制，使模型能动态调整计算量。

Abstract: Looped architectures provide an inductive bias toward learning step-by-step procedures for tasks that require compositional reasoning. The number of effective layers reached by looping determines the quality of the solution these models find. Like deep architectures, looped architectures are prone to a signal propagation problem induced by depth as the halting decision is postponed. In this paper, we address this signal propagation issue using pre-norm layers and residual scaling. Building on these architectural modifications, we propose FPRM, a Transformer-based Fixed-Point Reasoning Model that uses fixed-point convergence as an end-to-end halting mechanism in a looped architecture. We show that fixed-point halting allows FPRM to adapt its compute to task difficulty. FPRM is effective on common reasoning benchmarks, namely Sudoku, Maze, state-tracking, and ARC-AGI.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Zero-Shot Object-Goal Navigation (ZS-OGN) requires embodied agents to explore and locate target objects without any prior training. To this end, recent methods leverage foundation models. In this paper, we propose a self-evolving ZS-OGN framework that enables continuous test-time improvement. Specifically, we build an agentic rule memory by extracting actionable knowledge from past trajectories. Then, we propose a retrieval strategy based on upper confidence bound, selecting effective rules by balancing semantic relevance and historical success. In addition, we introduce a memory-guided preflection module that forecasts potential outcomes before action, reducing inefficient exploration. Extensive experiments show that our method outperforms existing zero-shot baselines, achieving a 10.1\% improvement in success rate with fewer unnecessary steps.

### [203] [Correct When Paired, Wrong When Split: Decoupling and Editing Modality-Specific Neurons in MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17057)
*Tingchao Fu,Wenkai Wang,Fanxiao Li,Huadong Zhang,Jinhong Zhang,Dayang Li,Yunyun Dong,Renyang Liu,Wei Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了多模态大模型（MLLMs）知识编辑中的编辑解耦失败问题，即在多模态输入下可更新实体知识，但在单模态输入时知识会回退到旧信息。通过实证分析发现，实体知识分散在不同模态特异的路径中，导致多模态更新无法有效传播至单模态通路。为此，作者提出DECODE方法，显式解耦并定位模态特异的神经元组，实现针对性的知识更新。大量实验表明，DECODE在不同模态触发下均能有效更新知识，显著缓解编辑解耦问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型的知识编辑方法在多模态输入下虽能更新知识，但在单模态输入时常出现知识回退，即编辑解耦失败。这一问题源于知识在模型中以模态特异的方式分布，导致更新无法跨模态有效传播。因此，亟需一种能够识别并针对特定模态路径进行精准编辑的方法。

Method: 提出DECODE方法，通过显式解耦和定位模态特异的神经元组，实现对不同模态路径的知识更新。该方法能够确保在多模态和单模态输入下均保持一致的更新效果，从而解决编辑解耦问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，DECODE在多种模态触发条件下均能稳定、有效地更新知识，显著降低编辑解耦失败率，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: DECODE成功解决了多模态大模型中因知识分布于不同模态路径而导致的编辑解耦问题，为实现跨模态一致的知识更新提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Although Knowledge Editing provides an efficient mechanism for updating the knowledge of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), we find that current paradigms still suffer from an important yet remain underexplored issue : editing decoupling failure, where entity-related knowledge can be updated when the model is triggered by multimodal inputs (text--image query pairs), however, it often reverts to outdated pre-edit facts when the paired inputs are split into unimodal ones. Our in-depth empirical analysis reveals that the entity knowledge in MLLMs is not stored as a unified representation, but is instead distributed across disentangled modality-specific pathways. As a result, updates biased toward multimodal queries fail to propagate effectively to unimodal circuits. To bridge this gap, we propose DECODE, which explicitly disentangles and localizes modality-specific neuron groups for targeted knowledge. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DECODE consistently achieves effective knowledge updates under different modality triggers, thereby mitigating editing decoupling failures.

</details>


### [204] [Diagnosing and Repairing Shape-Prior Shortcuts in Long-Range Single-Shot Fringe Projection Profilometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17093)
*Adam Haroon,Anush Lakshman,Cody Fleming,Beiwen Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对远距离（超过1米）单次投影条纹轮廓测量（FPP）中因强度衰减、相位信息缺失及现有学习模型机制不透明导致的性能瓶颈，提出了一种诊断-修复-验证框架。通过机制可解释性（MI）与保形不确定性量化（UQ）双重诊断，发现基准UNet模型依赖物体边界形状先验而非相位解码，从而误判任务本质。为此设计新型网络PhiCalNet，输出包裹相位并引入可微校准层映射至深度，从架构上排除形状先验路径。实验表明，PhiCalNet将平均绝对误差（MAE）降低3.3倍至4.46 mm，且残差主要集中在±π相位跳变点；保形UQ进一步验证了诊断结果：剔除5%不确定性最高的像素后，PhiCalNet的均方根误差（RMSE）下降64%（20.6→7.4 mm），而基线仅下降3.5%。MI与UQ在故障根源上达成一致，证实架构设计是关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远距离单次投影条纹轮廓测量面临逆平方强度衰减导致信噪比下降、物理真值退化、单图缺乏条纹序数信息使问题病态等挑战，且现有学习方法缺乏对内在机制的理解，亟需系统性的诊断与修复策略。

Method: 采用机制可解释性（MI）与保形不确定性量化（UQ）作为双轨诊断工具，结合线性探测、Grad-CAM可视化与平面外分布测试三类探针，定位模型错误根源；基于诊断结果重构网络架构，提出PhiCalNet，其输出包裹相位并通过固定可微校准层映射到深度，从架构层面消除形状先验依赖；同时设计物理信息损失进行对比验证。

Result: 在15,600张合成条纹图像（50个物体，1.5–2.1米距离）上，基准UNet MAE为14.54 mm；PhiCalNet将MAE降至4.46 mm（降幅3.3倍）；残差集中于±π相位跳变区域；保形UQ显示，剔除5%高不确定像素后，PhiCalNet RMSE下降64%（20.6→7.4 mm），显著优于基线（3.5%）。

Conclusion: 模型性能瓶颈的根本原因在于架构设计导致对形状先验的误用而非相位解码能力不足；通过架构层面的修复（PhiCalNet）可有效突破远距离单次FPP的性能极限；机制可解释性与不确定性量化协同诊断能精准定位物理失效根源，为复杂视觉任务的可信学习提供新范式。

Abstract: Learning-based single-shot fringe projection profilometry (FPP) has been studied mostly at close range. The long-range regime (standoff beyond 1 m) remains largely unaddressed: inverse-square intensity falloff lowers fringe signal-to-noise ratio and degrades physical ground truth, the single-shot problem is ill-posed because fringe-order information is absent from one image, and these architectures have not been studied mechanistically. We present a diagnose-repair-verify study using mechanistic interpretability (MI) and conformal uncertainty quantification (UQ) as convergent diagnostics: they agree on one physical failure locus, driving and verifying an architectural repair. On a photorealistic synthetic benchmark (15,600 fringe images, 50 objects at 1.5-2.1 m), a best UNet baseline reaches 14.54 mm object mean absolute error (MAE). Three probes (linear probing, Grad-CAM, flat-plane out-of-distribution test) converge: the baseline solves the task via object-boundary shape priors rather than fringe-phase decoding. We repair this with PhiCalNet, which outputs wrapped phase rather than depth and applies a fixed differentiable calibration layer mapping phase to depth, removing the shape-prior solution from the hypothesis space architecturally rather than by a loss penalty. A physics-informed loss that enforces the same physics as a soft penalty on a depth-regressing network yields no measurable gain, isolating the architecture as the operative factor. PhiCalNet reduces object MAE 3.3x to 4.46 mm; the residual is carried by 0.103% of pixels at the +/-pi wrap discontinuity. Pixel-wise conformal UQ confirms the diagnosis: rejecting the top 5% of object pixels by snapshot disagreement cuts PhiCalNet RMSE by 64% (20.6->7.4 mm) versus 3.5% for the baseline. MI and UQ converge on the same failure locus.

</details>


### [205] [Informative Missingness to Generate Irregular Clinical Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17106)
*Hadi Mehdizavareh,Gabriele Santangelo,Giovanna Nicora,Simon Lebech Cichosz,Arianna Dagliati,Arijit Khan,Riccardo Bellazzi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于扩散模型的方法，用于联合建模临床时间序列中的实验室数值及其观测模式。通过在MIMIC-III数据集基础上构建的DACMI基准上进行实验，该方法将图表时间对齐至4小时间隔，并将住院记录划分为7天窗口，生成包含每个检验值及其观测指示器的轨迹。模型扩展了TimeDiff框架，通过互补的扩散目标同时学习连续的检验值与离散的缺失模式，有效捕捉患者生理状态与临床检测行为之间的临床意义依赖关系，在MNAR（非随机缺失）情境下表现优异。生成数据在个体检验分布及值-缺失联合嵌入方面与真实患者轨迹高度一致，验证了扩散模型在建模信息性缺失方面的潜力，为构建临床基础模型提供合成先验支持，推动后续基于先验-数据拟合网络的训练研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验室检验数据的缺失并非随机，而是反映临床决策与患者生理状态的重要信息，传统处理方式将其视为预处理问题会丢失关键临床意义。因此需要直接建模缺失模式，以保留临床可解释性与数据真实性。

Method: 采用扩散模型框架，将时间序列对齐至4小时区间并分段为7天窗口，生成带观测指示的轨迹；使用标准变换与归一化稳定训练；扩展TimeDiff框架，设计互补扩散目标，分别学习连续检验值与离散缺失模式，实现联合建模。

Result: 生成数据在个体检验分布和值-缺失联合嵌入方面与真实数据高度匹配，表明模型能有效捕捉患者生理与检测行为间的临床依赖关系，尤其在非随机缺失（MNAR）场景下表现良好。

Conclusion: 该方法证明扩散模型可用于建模临床时间序列中信息性缺失，生成具有临床意义的合成数据，为构建临床基础模型提供可靠先验，未来可进一步用于训练能够利用缺失信息的Prior-Data Fitted Networks。

Abstract: Laboratory tests in electronic health records are collected irregularly, and the absence of a test order can be as informative as the measurement itself. Such missingness reflects clinicians' decisions and patient physiology, making it important to model it directly rather than treat it as a preprocessing artifact. Here we present a diffusion-based approach for generating clinical time series that jointly models laboratory values and their observation patterns using the public Data Analytics Challenge on Missing Data Imputation (DACMI) benchmark derived from MIMIC-III. To preserve realistic sampling, we align chart times into 4-hour intervals and segment admissions into 7-day windows, producing trajectories that pair each lab value with a corresponding observation indicator. Standard transformations and normalization are applied to stabilize training. Our method extends the TimeDiff framework to learn continuous lab values and discrete missingness patterns through complementary diffusion objectives. Experiments show that the generated data closely match real patient trajectories across individual lab distributions and joint value-missingness embeddings, demonstrating that diffusion models can capture clinically meaningful dependencies between patient physiology and clinicians' testing behavior under MNAR-like (missing-not-at-random) missingness. These preliminary results indicate that our model can serve as an initial component toward developing clinical foundation models. By producing synthetic priors that preserve key physiology-missingness relationships, this work motivates the subsequent training of Prior-Data Fitted Networks capable of leveraging informative missingness, which we will investigate in the extended work.

</details>


### [206] [Models Take Notes at Prefill: KV Cache Can Be Editable and Composable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17107)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种可编辑且可组合的前缀缓存机制，通过在预填充阶段重用共享前缀，同时支持对特定字段的修改与复用，实现低延迟推理。该方法利用模型已写入下游注意力的结论特性，仅更新关键字段即可恢复正确决策，并支持跨上下文拼接技能，显著降低计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前缀缓存因任一字段变化即失效，导致效率低下；同时无法有效支持动态编辑与复用。本文旨在解决这一瓶颈，提升缓存利用率和推理灵活性。

Method: 基于因果分析发现模型在预填充时已将条件性结论写入下游注意权重，因此只需替换关键字段的键值向量，其余部分可复用。结合链式思维（CoT）实现编辑，通过旋转位置编码（RoPE）实现技能的可组合性，构建统一的编辑+组合代理。

Result: 在12个模型上验证，日志余弦相似度达0.90-0.999，延迟降低最高至14.9倍；在线vLLM基准中，前缀缓存命中率达98.5%，p90首次生成时间减少53-398倍。适用于多种架构与注意力变体。

Conclusion: 所提方法实现了高效、可编辑、可组合的前缀缓存，既保持与完整重计算一致的决策性能，又大幅降低延迟，具备广泛适用性与生产部署潜力。

Abstract: Prefix caching reuses prefill only across an exactly shared prefix, so one changed field invalidates the entire downstream cache. Yet overwriting the field's own key/value vectors and reusing the rest leaves the model acting on the old value. The reason, established causally across four model families: at prefill the model has already written the field-conditioned conclusion onto downstream notes; the field's own key/value drives under 1% of the decision. Read as a notebook of memoized conclusions, two capabilities follow. (1) It is editable. A salient erratum amends the notes; and with chain-of-thought, editing the field alone recovers the decision (1.00 at 8B, ~1% compute), while without CoT it is ignored. (2) It is composable. The notes are position-portable, so a precompiled skill can be RoPE-repositioned and spliced into any context, indistinguishable from full recompute (logit cosine 0.90-0.999, twelve models) at O(L) rather than O(L^2) time-to-first-token. A unified edit+compose agent stays decision-identical to recompute at up to 14.9x lower latency. The approach applies to any per-token attention KV cache, validated across scale, quantization, Mixture-of-Experts, and multimodal caches, and extends to several attention variants through small adapters. Because the erratum is append-only, it composes with production prefix caching: in an online vLLM benchmark it keeps the prefix cache-aligned (98.5% hit-rate), cutting p90 time-to-first-token by 53-398x.

</details>


### [207] [The Critical Role of Model Selection in Causal Inference: A Comparative Analysis of Classification Models within the InferBERT Framework for Pharmacovigilance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17113)
*Csaba Kiss,Roland Molontay,Gabriele Pergola*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究评估了InferBERT框架中不同模型选择对因果药物不良事件检测的影响，发现领域特定预训练的BioBERT在准确率和与传统信号的一致性上表现最佳，而更大的医学大模型Med-LLaMA表现不佳。结果表明，领域专用模型比简单基线或更大规模的LLM更有效，强调了针对性预训练的重要性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在药物警戒中，区分因果性药物不良事件与虚假相关性仍是核心挑战。现有方法如InferBERT依赖于底层分类模型的表现，因此需系统评估模型选择的影响，以优化因果推理性能。

Method: 采用5折交叉验证重复20次，对比XGBoost、ALBERT、BioBERT和Med-LLaMA四种模型在阿司匹林诱导急性肝衰竭（AILF）和曲马多相关死亡（TRAM）两个基准数据集上的表现，评估指标包括准确率、预期校准误差（ECE）以及与PRR、ROR、EBGM等传统信号的Jaccard一致性，并使用配对t检验进行显著性分析。

Result: BioBERT在两个数据集上均达到最高准确率，且与传统药警信号具有最强的Jaccard一致性；尽管参数量大，但Med-LLaMA表现较差；领域特定预训练显著提升性能；后处理校准改善了ECE，但对准确率和因果发现影响不一。

Conclusion: 领域特定预训练的中小型模型（如BioBERT）在计算药警中优于简单基线和大规模医学LLM，表明投资于可管理、领域感知的模型比单纯扩大模型规模更为有效。

Abstract: Distinguishing causal adverse drug events (ADEs) from spurious correlations remains a central challenge in pharmacovigilance. The InferBERT framework integrates transformer models with Do-calculus, but its success hinges on the underlying classification model. This study evaluates the impact of model choice in InferBERT, assessing whether simpler models suffice, if domain-specific pre-training helps, whether scaling to LLMs improves causal detection, and the effect of post-hoc calibration. We performed a comparative study on two benchmarks: Analgesics-induced Acute Liver Failure (AILF) and Tramadol-related Mortalities (TRAM). Four models were evaluated-XGBoost (baseline), ALBERT (original InferBERT), BioBERT (biomedical transformer), and Med-LLaMA (medical LLM)-using 5-fold cross-validation repeated over 20 runs. We measured accuracy, Expected Calibration Error (ECE) pre- and post-isotonic regression, and Jaccard concordance of causal terms with PRR, ROR, and EBGM; significance was tested with paired t-tests. BioBERT achieved the highest accuracy on both datasets, while Med-LLaMA underperformed despite its size and parameter-efficient fine-tuning. Domain-specific pre-training was decisive. Calibration improved ECE but had mixed effects on accuracy and causal discovery. BioBERT's superiority also yielded the strongest concordance with traditional pharmacovigilance signals. These results show that domain-specific pre-training provides a clear advantage over simpler baselines and larger LLMs. Investing in manageable, domain-aware models is more effective for computational pharmacovigilance than simply scaling model size.

Our results show that FM representations achieve competitive performance on out-of-distribution data and that multimodal fusion helps mainly when no single modality dominates the signal. ### [209] [MODE: Modality-Decomposed Expert-Level Mixed-Precision Quantization for MoE Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17118)
*Yuanteng Chen,Peisong Wang,Zhilei Liu,Nanxin Zeng,Yuantian Shao,Shiqiang Lang,Tao Liu,Chuangyi Li,Qinghao Hu,Gang Li,Jing Liu,Jian Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MODE提出了一种针对Mixture-of-Experts Multimodal Large Language Models（MoE-MLLMs）的模态分解式专家级混合精度量化框架，通过解耦不同模态的专家选择频率、过滤冗余视觉令牌并结合模态感知的量化敏感度评估，有效缓解了现有方法在跨模态和视觉内部偏差下的性能下降问题。该方法基于整数线性规划分配每专家比特宽度，在保持低内存开销的同时显著提升压缩效率与模型性能，尤其在2位设置下表现优异，平均性能损失控制在2.9%以内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有专家级混合精度量化方法在MoE-MLLMs上表现不佳，主要由于两个未被充分考虑的偏差：一是跨模态中视觉令牌数量占优导致专家选择频率被视觉主导，掩盖了对文本模态关键的专家；二是视觉内部存在大量冗余令牌，进一步扭曲频率统计，使得重要视觉内容对应的专家难以被识别。因此需要一种能区分模态影响、去除噪声并精准评估专家重要性的新方法。

Method: 提出MODE框架，包括：1）按模态分解专家选择频率，分离视觉与文本模态的影响；2）设计去噪机制过滤冗余视觉令牌，获得更纯净的视觉频率分布；3）引入模态特异性量化敏感度作为补充信号，增强重要性评估；4）将频率与敏感度信号整合进整数线性规划模型，以在给定比特预算下最优分配各专家的位宽。

Result: 实验表明，MODE在W3A16设置下平均性能损失低于2.9%，在极端2比特设置下性能提升更为显著，验证了其对MoE-MLLMs的有效性与优越性，尤其在降低内存占用同时保持高保真度方面表现突出。

Conclusion: MODE通过模态解耦与多信号融合的量化策略，有效解决了现有混合精度量化方法在多模态场景中的偏差问题，为MoE-MLLMs的高效压缩提供了可靠方案，具有良好的实用价值与推广潜力。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts Multimodal Large Language Models (MoE-MLLMs) offer remarkable performance but incur prohibitive GPU memory costs, making compression essential. Among PTQ methods, expert-level mixed-precision quantization has proven effective for MoE-LLMs, yet suffers notable degradation on MoE-MLLMs due to two overlooked biases in expert importance estimation. (1) At the cross-modal level, the numerical dominance of vision tokens causes expert selection frequency to be dominated by vision tokens, masking experts that are critical to the text modality; (2) at the intra-vision level, the large proportion of redundant vision tokens further skew frequency statistics, obscuring experts critical for informative visual content. To bridge gaps, we propose MODE, a modality-decomposed expert-level mixed-precision quantization framework for MoE-MLLMs that decomposes expert selection frequency by modality, filters redundant vision tokens to obtain denoised visual frequency, and further evaluates quantization sensitivity per modality as a complementary signal to frequency-based estimation. These signals are integrated into an Integer Linear Programming formulation to assign per-expert bit-widths under a given budget. Extensive experiments show that MODE is particularly well-suited for MoE-MLLMs, limiting average performance loss to within 2.9% at W3A16, with larger gains at the extreme 2-bit setting.

### [210] [Noise-Driven Escape from Metastable Phases explains Grokking in Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17120)
*Ibrahim Talha Ersoy,Karoline Wiesner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了线性深度神经网络（DNN）在L2正则化强度变化下出现的一阶相变现象，这些相变标志着新可学习特征的开启。当正则化强度低于临界值时，所有特征理论上均可学习，但存在多个由能量壁垒分隔的亚稳态，可能导致模型陷入局部最优并阻碍收敛。研究发现，'grokking'——即长期过拟合后突然出现的泛化能力——与一阶相变中的滞后效应一致。通过人为引入陷阱，利用随机梯度下降（SGD）噪声驱动模型穿越能量壁垒，实现延迟收敛，其逃逸时间符合阿伦尼乌斯定律。通过稀疏子采样，成功复现了典型的grokking曲线，测试误差最终趋近于训练误差。研究提出，亚稳态数量等于可学习特征数（即数据协方差矩阵的奇异值个数），任务复杂度越高，滞后效应越显著。证据表明该机制可能也适用于一般非线性DNN，为更高效的训练方法提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解深度神经网络中'grokking'现象的起源，即模型在经历长时间过拟合后突然实现泛化，是当前机器学习中的关键开放问题之一。已有研究表明，DNN在正则化强度变化下会出现一阶相变，这提示可能存在与亚稳态和能量壁垒相关的物理机制。因此，本研究旨在探索相变与grokking之间的联系，揭示其背后的动力学原理。

Method: 采用线性深度神经网络模型，系统分析不同L2正则化强度下的学习行为；通过设计特定的正则化策略制造人为的亚稳态陷阱；利用随机梯度下降（SGD）的固有噪声作为驱动力，模拟模型从亚稳态逃逸的过程；测量逃逸时间并验证其是否符合阿伦尼乌斯定律；通过稀疏子采样构建类似真实任务的数据集，重现grokking曲线。

Result: 成功在人工设置的亚稳态中观察到延迟收敛现象，逃逸时间跨越两个数量级且服从阿伦尼乌斯规律；稀疏子采样下再现典型grokking曲线，测试误差随时间下降并逼近训练误差；证实亚稳态数量与数据协方差的奇异值数量一致，表明每个可学习特征对应一个亚稳态；推断该机制可能普遍存在于非线性DNN中。

Conclusion: grokking现象可被解释为一阶相变中的滞后效应，由亚稳态和能量壁垒引起。通过控制正则化可人为诱导模型陷入亚稳态，并借助SGD噪声实现延迟逃逸。这一机制不仅解释了grokking，还揭示了模型复杂性与学习动力学之间的深层联系，为设计更高效、更稳定的训练算法提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) exhibit first order phase transitions under variations of the L2 regularization strength, with each transition marking the onset of a new learnable feature. Below a critical regularization strength, all features are in principle learnable, but coexisting metastable states, separated by energy barriers, can trap the network and impede convergence. A strength of DNNs is their ability to generalize. But many open questions remain, among them the origin of so called grokking: the abrupt, delayed onset of generalization after prolonged apparent overfitting. We show for linear DNNs that grokking is consistent with hysteresis in first-order L2 phase transitions: using L2 regularization to engineer deliberate trapping, we demonstrate that a model in a low-accuracy metastable state escapes only when SGD noise drives it across an energy barrier, with escape times following Arrhenius scaling. We reproduce grokking-like delayed convergence across two orders of magnitude in escape time by deliberately trapping models in metastable phases. Using sparse sub-sampling we also reproduce the canonical grokking curve where test error eventually approaches the final training error. Our work suggests that the number of metastable states equals the number of learnable features -- one per singular value of the data covariance -- the potential for hysteresis grows naturally with task complexity. We provide evidence that the same mechanism likely operates in general nonlinear DNNs. Our results provide routes toward more efficient learning schemes.

</details>
